#!/usr/bin/env python3
from __future__ import annotations

from pathlib import Path

ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parent

PROJECT_FILES = [

  'runtime_backend/tests/test_commands.py',
  'runtime_backend/tests/test_startup_probe.py',
]


def ensure_project_structure() -> tuple[int, int]:
  created_dirs = 0
  created_files = 0

  for relative_path in PROJECT_FILES:
    file_path = ROOT / relative_path
    parent_dir = file_path.parent

    if parent_dir != ROOT:
      missing_chain: list[Path] = []
      current = parent_dir

      while current != ROOT and not current.exists():
        missing_chain.append(current)
        current = current.parent

      if missing_chain:
        parent_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        created_dirs += len(missing_chain)

    if not file_path.exists():
      file_path.touch()
      created_files += 1

  return created_dirs, created_files


def main() -> None:
  created_dirs, created_files = ensure_project_structure()
  print(
    'Project structure is ready. '
    f'Created directories: {created_dirs}, created files: {created_files}.'
  )


if __name__ == '__main__':
  main()

def export_files() -> None:
  lines: list[str] = []
  lines.append('=' * 50)
  lines.append('PROJECT EXPORT')
  lines.append('=' * 50)
  lines.append('')

  for relative_path in PROJECT_FILES:
    file_path = ROOT / relative_path

    lines.append('=' * 50)
    lines.append(f'FILE: {relative_path}')
    lines.append('=' * 50)
    lines.append('')

    if not file_path.exists():
      lines.append('[FILE NOT FOUND]')
      lines.append('')
      continue

    try:
      content = file_path.read_text(encoding='utf-8')
    except UnicodeDecodeError:
      content = file_path.read_text(encoding='utf-8', errors='replace')

    lines.append(content)
    lines.append('')

  OUTPUT_FILE.write_text('\n'.join(lines), encoding='utf-8')
  print(f'Export finished: {OUTPUT_FILE}')


if __name__ == '__main__':
  export_files()

import { app, BrowserWindow, ipcMain, dialog, Menu, nativeImage } from 'electron';
import fs from 'node:fs/promises';
import path from 'node:path';
import { APP_CONFIG } from './config/app-config.js';
import { createWindowCloseGuard } from './main/runtime/windowCloseGuard.js';

function createAppMenu(mainWindow) {
  const sendAction = (action) => {
    if (!mainWindow.isDestroyed()) {
      mainWindow.webContents.send(APP_CONFIG.platform.app.menu.menuEventChannel, action);
    }
  };
  const menuConfig = APP_CONFIG.platform.app.menu;
  const menuIconAssetsByAction = APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.assets.menuByAction;
  const MENU_ICON_SIZE = APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.nativeMenuSmall;
  const PUBLIC_ICONS_BROWSER_PREFIX = '/icons/';
  const PUBLIC_ICONS_FS_ROOT = path.join(process.cwd(), 'public', 'icons');
  const browserIconPathToFsPath = (browserIconPath) => {
    if (typeof browserIconPath !== 'string' || !browserIconPath.startsWith(PUBLIC_ICONS_BROWSER_PREFIX)) {
      return undefined;
    }

    const iconFileName = browserIconPath.slice(PUBLIC_ICONS_BROWSER_PREFIX.length);

    if (!iconFileName) {
      return undefined;
    }

    return path.join(PUBLIC_ICONS_FS_ROOT, iconFileName);
  };
  const resolveMenuIcon = (actionKey) => {
    const browserPath = menuIconAssetsByAction[actionKey];
    const fsIconPath = browserIconPathToFsPath(browserPath);

    if (!fsIconPath) {
      return undefined;
    }

    const menuIconImage = nativeImage.createFromPath(fsIconPath);

    if (menuIconImage.isEmpty()) {
      return undefined;
    }

    return menuIconImage.resize({
      width: MENU_ICON_SIZE,
      height: MENU_ICON_SIZE
    });
  };

  const template = [
    {
      label: menuConfig.fileLabel,
      submenu: [
        {
          label: menuConfig.items.newProject,
          icon: resolveMenuIcon('newProject'),
          click: () => sendAction(menuConfig.actionIds.newProject)
        },
        {
          label: menuConfig.items.openProject,
          icon: resolveMenuIcon('openProject'),
          click: () => sendAction(menuConfig.actionIds.openProject)
        },
        {
          label: menuConfig.items.closeProject,
          icon: resolveMenuIcon('closeProject'),
          click: () => sendAction(menuConfig.actionIds.closeProject)
        },
        { type: 'separator' },
        {
          label: menuConfig.items.save,
          icon: resolveMenuIcon('save'),
          click: () => sendAction(menuConfig.actionIds.save)
        },
        {
          label: menuConfig.items.saveAs,
          icon: resolveMenuIcon('saveAs'),
          click: () => sendAction(menuConfig.actionIds.saveAs)
        },
        { type: 'separator' },
        {
          label: menuConfig.items.exit,
          icon: resolveMenuIcon('exit'),
          click: () => sendAction(menuConfig.actionIds.exit)
        }
      ]
    }
  ];

  const menu = Menu.buildFromTemplate(template);
  Menu.setApplicationMenu(menu);
}

let mainWindow = null;
const windowCloseGuard = createWindowCloseGuard();

function createWindow() {
  const win = new BrowserWindow({
    width: APP_CONFIG.platform.window.width,
    height: APP_CONFIG.platform.window.height,
    webPreferences: {
      contextIsolation: true,
      nodeIntegration: false,
      preload: path.join(process.cwd(), 'preload.cjs')
    }
  });

  createAppMenu(win);

  win.webContents.on('before-input-event', (_event, input) => {
    if (input.type !== 'keyDown') {
      return;
    }

    const isCtrlShiftI = input.control && input.shift && String(input.key).toLowerCase() === 'i';

    if (isCtrlShiftI) {
      win.webContents.openDevTools({ mode: 'detach' });
    }
  });

  win.on('close', (event) => {
    const decision = windowCloseGuard.handleCloseAttempt({
      isWindowDestroyed: win.isDestroyed()
    });

    if (decision.preventDefault) {
      event.preventDefault();
    }

    if (decision.requestRendererConfirmation) {
      win.webContents.send(APP_CONFIG.platform.ipc.channels.windowCloseRequested);
    }
  });

  win.on('closed', () => {
    if (mainWindow === win) {
      mainWindow = null;
      windowCloseGuard.reset();
    }
  });

  win.loadURL(APP_CONFIG.platform.window.devServerUrl);
  return win;
}

app.whenReady().then(() => {
  ipcMain.handle(APP_CONFIG.platform.ipc.handlers.openProjectDialog, async () => {
    const result = await dialog.showOpenDialog({
      title: APP_CONFIG.platform.app.dialogs.openProjectTitle,
      properties: ['openFile'],
      filters: [
        {
          name: APP_CONFIG.platform.app.dialogs.projectFilterName,
          extensions: APP_CONFIG.platform.app.dialogs.yamlFilterExtensions
        }
      ]
    });

    if (result.canceled || !result.filePaths[0]) {
      return null;
    }

    return result.filePaths[0];
  });

  ipcMain.handle(APP_CONFIG.platform.ipc.handlers.saveProjectAsDialog, async (_event, defaultPath) => {
    const result = await dialog.showSaveDialog({
      title: APP_CONFIG.platform.app.dialogs.saveProjectAsTitle,
      defaultPath,
      buttonLabel: APP_CONFIG.platform.app.dialogs.saveButtonLabel,
      filters: [
        {
          name: APP_CONFIG.platform.app.dialogs.yamlFilterName,
          extensions: APP_CONFIG.platform.app.dialogs.yamlFilterExtensions
        }
      ]
    });

    if (result.canceled || !result.filePath) {
      return null;
    }

    return result.filePath;
  });

  ipcMain.handle(APP_CONFIG.platform.ipc.handlers.saveBinaryFileAsDialog, async (_event, options = {}) => {
    const defaultPath = typeof options?.defaultPath === 'string' ? options.defaultPath : undefined;
    const title = typeof options?.title === 'string' ? options.title : APP_CONFIG.platform.app.dialogs.exportProjectArchiveTitle;
    const buttonLabel = typeof options?.buttonLabel === 'string' ? options.buttonLabel : APP_CONFIG.platform.app.dialogs.exportButtonLabel;
    const filters = Array.isArray(options?.filters) && options.filters.length
      ? options.filters
      : [
          {
            name: APP_CONFIG.platform.app.dialogs.zipFilterName,
            extensions: APP_CONFIG.platform.app.dialogs.zipFilterExtensions
          }
        ];

    const result = await dialog.showSaveDialog({
      title,
      defaultPath,
      buttonLabel,
      filters
    });

    if (result.canceled || !result.filePath) {
      return {
        saved: false,
        filePath: null
      };
    }

    const bytes = options?.bytes;
    const binaryBuffer = ArrayBuffer.isView(bytes)
      ? Buffer.from(bytes.buffer, bytes.byteOffset, bytes.byteLength)
      : Array.isArray(bytes)
        ? Buffer.from(bytes)
        : Buffer.alloc(0);
    await fs.mkdir(path.dirname(result.filePath), { recursive: true });
    await fs.writeFile(result.filePath, binaryBuffer);

    return {
      saved: true,
      filePath: result.filePath
    };
  });

  ipcMain.handle(APP_CONFIG.platform.ipc.handlers.appQuit, async () => {
    windowCloseGuard.approveClose();
    app.quit();
    return true;
  });

  ipcMain.handle(APP_CONFIG.platform.ipc.handlers.windowCloseApproved, async () => {
    if (!mainWindow || mainWindow.isDestroyed()) {
      return false;
    }

    windowCloseGuard.approveClose();
    mainWindow.close();
    return true;
  });

  ipcMain.handle(APP_CONFIG.platform.ipc.handlers.windowCloseCancelled, async () => {
    windowCloseGuard.cancelClose();
    return true;
  });

  ipcMain.handle(APP_CONFIG.platform.ipc.handlers.fsEnsureDir, async (_event, targetPath) => {
    await fs.mkdir(targetPath, { recursive: true });
    return true;
  });

  ipcMain.handle(APP_CONFIG.platform.ipc.handlers.fsExists, async (_event, targetPath) => {
    try {
      await fs.access(targetPath);
      return true;
    } catch {
      return false;
    }
  });

  ipcMain.handle(APP_CONFIG.platform.ipc.handlers.fsReadText, async (_event, targetPath) => {
    return fs.readFile(targetPath, 'utf-8');
  });

  ipcMain.handle(APP_CONFIG.platform.ipc.handlers.fsWriteText, async (_event, targetPath, text) => {
    await fs.mkdir(path.dirname(targetPath), { recursive: true });
    await fs.writeFile(targetPath, text, 'utf-8');
    return true;
  });

  ipcMain.handle(APP_CONFIG.platform.ipc.handlers.fsRename, async (_event, fromPath, toPath) => {
    await fs.mkdir(path.dirname(toPath), { recursive: true });
    await fs.rename(fromPath, toPath);
    return true;
  });

  ipcMain.handle(APP_CONFIG.platform.ipc.handlers.fsDeleteFile, async (_event, targetPath) => {
    await fs.rm(targetPath, { force: true });
    return true;
  });

  ipcMain.handle(APP_CONFIG.platform.ipc.handlers.fsDeleteDir, async (_event, targetPath) => {
    await fs.rm(targetPath, { recursive: true, force: true });
    return true;
  });

  ipcMain.handle(APP_CONFIG.platform.ipc.handlers.fsListFiles, async (_event, targetDir, extensions = []) => {
    const output = [];

    async function walk(currentDir) {
      const entries = await fs.readdir(currentDir, { withFileTypes: true });

      for (const entry of entries) {
        const fullPath = path.join(currentDir, entry.name);

        if (entry.isDirectory()) {
          await walk(fullPath);
          continue;
        }

        if (!extensions.length) {
          output.push(fullPath);
          continue;
        }

        const normalized = entry.name.toLowerCase();

        if (extensions.some((ext) => normalized.endsWith(ext.toLowerCase()))) {
          output.push(fullPath);
        }
      }
    }

    const exists = await fs.access(targetDir).then(() => true).catch(() => false);

    if (!exists) {
      return [];
    }

    await walk(targetDir);
    return output;
  });

  mainWindow = createWindow();
});

app.on('window-all-closed', () => {
  if (process.platform !== APP_CONFIG.platform.runtime.mac) {
    app.quit();
  }
});

const { contextBridge, ipcRenderer } = require('electron');

const IPC = {
  channels: {
    menuAction: 'menu:action',
    windowCloseRequested: 'window:close-requested'
  },
  handlers: {
    openProjectDialog: 'dialog:open-project',
    saveProjectAsDialog: 'dialog:save-project-as',
    saveBinaryFileAsDialog: 'dialog:save-binary-file-as',
    appQuit: 'app:quit',
    windowCloseApproved: 'window:close-approved',
    windowCloseCancelled: 'window:close-cancelled',
    fsEnsureDir: 'fs:ensure-dir',
    fsExists: 'fs:exists',
    fsReadText: 'fs:read-text',
    fsWriteText: 'fs:write-text',
    fsRename: 'fs:rename',
    fsDeleteFile: 'fs:delete-file',
    fsDeleteDir: 'fs:delete-dir',
    fsListFiles: 'fs:list-files'
  }
};

contextBridge.exposeInMainWorld('MetaPlatformFS', {
  openProjectFileDialog: () => ipcRenderer.invoke(IPC.handlers.openProjectDialog),
  saveProjectFileAsDialog: (defaultPath) => ipcRenderer.invoke(IPC.handlers.saveProjectAsDialog, defaultPath),
  saveBinaryFileAsDialog: (options) => ipcRenderer.invoke(IPC.handlers.saveBinaryFileAsDialog, options),
  requestAppQuit: () => ipcRenderer.invoke(IPC.handlers.appQuit),
  approveWindowClose: () => ipcRenderer.invoke(IPC.handlers.windowCloseApproved),
  cancelWindowClose: () => ipcRenderer.invoke(IPC.handlers.windowCloseCancelled),
  ensureDir: (targetPath) => ipcRenderer.invoke(IPC.handlers.fsEnsureDir, targetPath),
  exists: (targetPath) => ipcRenderer.invoke(IPC.handlers.fsExists, targetPath),
  readText: (targetPath) => ipcRenderer.invoke(IPC.handlers.fsReadText, targetPath),
  writeText: (targetPath, text) => ipcRenderer.invoke(IPC.handlers.fsWriteText, targetPath, text),
  rename: (fromPath, toPath) => ipcRenderer.invoke(IPC.handlers.fsRename, fromPath, toPath),
  deleteFile: (targetPath) => ipcRenderer.invoke(IPC.handlers.fsDeleteFile, targetPath),
  deleteDir: (targetPath) => ipcRenderer.invoke(IPC.handlers.fsDeleteDir, targetPath),
  listFiles: (targetDir, extensions) => ipcRenderer.invoke(IPC.handlers.fsListFiles, targetDir, extensions),

  onWindowCloseRequested: (listener) => {
    const wrapped = () => listener();
    ipcRenderer.on(IPC.channels.windowCloseRequested, wrapped);
    return () => ipcRenderer.off(IPC.channels.windowCloseRequested, wrapped);
  },

  onMenuAction: (listener) => {
    const wrapped = (_event, action) => listener(action);
    const menuEventChannel = IPC.channels.menuAction;
    ipcRenderer.on(menuEventChannel, wrapped);
    return () => ipcRenderer.off(menuEventChannel, wrapped);
  }
});

import { applyStaticText } from './ui/applyStaticText.js';
import { createCoreLogger } from './core/logger.js';
import { createCommandBus } from './core/commandBus.js';
import { createModuleRegistry } from './core/moduleRegistry.js';
import { createProjectManager } from './core/projectManager.js';
import { createFileSystemBridge } from './runtime/fileSystemBridge.js';
import { initWorkbenchLayout } from './core/layout.js';
import { createWorkbenchTabs } from './ui/createWorkbenchTabs.js';
import { createProjectTree } from './ui/createProjectTree.js';
import { showSaveChangesDialog, showTextInputDialog } from './ui/dialogs.js';
import { getDocumentIdentityKey } from './runtime/documentRecordIdentity.js';
import { createAppCloseCoordinator } from './runtime/appCloseCoordinator.js';
import { createConsoleLogSink, createDomLogSink } from './core/loggerSinks.js';
import { METAGEN_CONFIG } from './modules/metagen/metagenConfig.js';

import { createMetaGenModule } from './modules/metagen/metagenModule.js';
import { createMetaLabModule } from './modules/metalab/metalabModule.js';
import { createMetaViewModule } from './modules/metaview/metaviewModule.js';
import { APP_CONFIG } from '../config/app-config.js';
import { buildProjectFilePath } from './runtime/projectPaths.js';
import { setNodeIconAndText } from './ui/pngIconRenderer.js';
import { createRuntimeClient } from './runtime/runtimeClient.js';
import { createHttpRuntimeAdapter } from './runtime/adapters/createHttpRuntimeAdapter.js';
import { runBackendProjectExport } from './runtime/backendProjectExportFlow.js';

export function getCurrentBackendProjectId({ projectManager, backendSource }) {
  const project = projectManager?.getCurrentProject?.();
  if (!project || project.source !== backendSource) {
    return '';
  }

  return String(
    project.backendProject?.projectId
    || project.project?.id
    || ''
  ).trim();
}

export async function closeDeletedBackendProjectIfOpened({
  projectId,
  projectManager,
  backendSource,
  tabs,
  logger,
  tree
}) {
  const normalizedProjectId = String(projectId || '').trim();
  if (!normalizedProjectId) {
    return false;
  }

  const currentBackendProjectId = getCurrentBackendProjectId({
    projectManager,
    backendSource
  });
  if (!currentBackendProjectId || currentBackendProjectId !== normalizedProjectId) {
    return false;
  }

  try {
    await tabs.closeAllTabs();
  } catch (_error) {
    // Continue close flow even if one tab fails to close cleanly.
  }
  logger.clear();
  await projectManager?.closeProject?.();
  await tree.render();
  return true;
}

export async function deleteBackendProjectFlow({
  project,
  confirmDelete,
  confirmPrefix,
  deleteCommandId,
  executeBackendCommand,
  closeDeletedProject,
  refreshBackendProjects
}) {
  const projectId = String(project?.id || '').trim();
  if (!projectId) {
    return false;
  }

  const projectLabel = `${project?.name || projectId}`;
  const confirmed = confirmDelete(`${confirmPrefix} ${projectLabel}`);
  if (!confirmed) {
    return false;
  }

  const result = await executeBackendCommand(deleteCommandId, { projectId });
  if (!result) {
    return false;
  }

  await closeDeletedProject(projectId);
  await refreshBackendProjects();
  return true;
}

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', async () => {
  applyStaticText();

  const logger = createCoreLogger({
    sinks: [
      createDomLogSink({ output: document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.logContainerId) }),
      createConsoleLogSink()
    ]
  });
  const commandBus = createCommandBus({ logger });
  const moduleRegistry = createModuleRegistry({ logger });
  const fileSystem = createFileSystemBridge();
  const workbenchLayout = initWorkbenchLayout();
  const backendRuntimeClient = createRuntimeClient({
    adapter: createHttpRuntimeAdapter({
      baseUrl: APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.baseUrl,
      endpointPath: APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandsEndpoint,
      timeoutMs: APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.requestTimeoutMs,
      errorCodes: {
        internal: APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.errorCodes.internal
      }
    })
  });

  window.MetaPlatformRuntime = window.MetaPlatformRuntime || {};

  let projectManager = null;
  const getProjectManager = () => projectManager;

  const metaGenModule = createMetaGenModule({ logger, getProjectManager });
  const metaLabModule = createMetaLabModule({ logger, getProjectManager });
  const metaViewModule = createMetaViewModule({ logger, getProjectManager });

  moduleRegistry.registerModule(metaGenModule);
  moduleRegistry.registerModule(metaLabModule);
  moduleRegistry.registerModule(metaViewModule);

  const paramsUndoButton = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.paramsUndoButtonId);
  const paramsRedoButton = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.paramsRedoButtonId);
  let disposeParamsUndoRedoSubscription = null;

  const tabs = createWorkbenchTabs({
    logger,
    onActiveEntryChanged: () => {
      disposeParamsUndoRedoSubscription?.();
      disposeParamsUndoRedoSubscription = null;

      const runtime = tabs.getActiveRuntime?.();
      if (typeof runtime?.subscribeParamsUndoRedoState === 'function') {
        disposeParamsUndoRedoSubscription = runtime.subscribeParamsUndoRedoState(() => {
          updateParamsUndoRedoButtonsState();
        });
      }

      updateParamsUndoRedoButtonsState();
    },
    projectManager: {
      renameDocument: async (...args) => projectManager?.renameDocument(...args),
      replaceDocumentRecord: async (...args) => projectManager?.replaceDocumentRecord(...args)
    },
    openEditor: async ({ documentRecord, mountElement }) => {
      const module = moduleRegistry.findModuleByDocumentKind(documentRecord.document?.kind);

      if (!module) {
        throw new Error(`Не найден модуль для kind=${documentRecord.document?.kind}`);
      }

      const runtime = await module.openDocument({
        documentRecord,
        mountElement,
        onDirty: () => projectManager?.markDocumentDirty(getDocumentIdentityKey(documentRecord))
      });

      decorateEditorPanelHeaders(mountElement);
      return runtime;
    }
  });

  function decorateEditorPanelHeaders(rootNode) {
    const headerIconByLabel = new Map([
      [APP_CONFIG.ui.panelHeaders.params, APP_CONFIG.ui.panelHeaderIcons.params],
      [APP_CONFIG.ui.panelHeaders.data, APP_CONFIG.ui.panelHeaderIcons.data],
      [APP_CONFIG.ui.panelHeaders.code, APP_CONFIG.ui.panelHeaderIcons.code],
      [METAGEN_CONFIG.ui.panelHeaders.instances, METAGEN_CONFIG.ui.panelHeaderIcons.instances]
    ]);
    const headerSelector = `.${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.editorPanelHeader}`;
    const headerNodes = rootNode.querySelectorAll?.(headerSelector) || [];

    for (const headerNode of headerNodes) {
      const normalizedText = String(headerNode.textContent || '').trim();
      const iconAssetPath = headerIconByLabel.get(normalizedText);
      if (!iconAssetPath) {
        continue;
      }

      setNodeIconAndText(headerNode, {
        iconAssetPath,
        labelText: normalizedText,
        textClassName: APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.panelHeaderText
      });
    }
  }

  const backendCatalogNode = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.backendPanelId);
  const backendListButton = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.backendListButtonId);
  const backendCreateInput = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.backendCreateInputId);
  const backendCreateButton = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.backendCreateButtonId);
  const backendResultNode = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.backendResultId);
  let backendRequestCounter = 0;

  if (backendCatalogNode) {
    backendCatalogNode.querySelector(`.${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendPanelHeader}`)?.replaceChildren(APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectsTitle);
  }

  if (backendListButton) {
    backendListButton.textContent = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendListProjects;
  }

  if (backendCreateInput) {
    backendCreateInput.placeholder = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectPlaceholder;
  }

  if (backendCreateButton) {
    backendCreateButton.textContent = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendCreateProject;
  }

  function setBackendResult(value) {
    if (!backendResultNode) {
      return;
    }

    backendResultNode.replaceChildren(
      typeof value === 'string'
        ? document.createTextNode(value)
        : document.createTextNode(JSON.stringify(value, null, 2))
    );
  }

  function renderBackendProjects(projects = []) {
    if (!backendResultNode) {
      return;
    }

    backendResultNode.replaceChildren();

    if (!Array.isArray(projects) || projects.length === 0) {
      backendResultNode.appendChild(document.createTextNode('[]'));
      return;
    }

    for (const project of projects) {
      const row = document.createElement('div');
      const label = document.createElement('span');
      const openButton = document.createElement('button');
      const exportButton = document.createElement('button');
      const deleteButton = document.createElement('button');
      const projectLabel = `${project?.name || ''} (${project?.slug || ''})`;

      label.textContent = projectLabel;
      openButton.type = 'button';
      openButton.textContent = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendOpenProject;
      openButton.addEventListener('click', () => {
        void openBackendProject(project);
      });
      exportButton.type = 'button';
      exportButton.textContent = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendExportProject;
      exportButton.addEventListener('click', () => {
        void exportBackendProject(project);
      });
      deleteButton.type = 'button';
      deleteButton.textContent = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendDeleteProject;
      deleteButton.addEventListener('click', () => {
        void deleteBackendProject(project);
      });

      row.append(
        label,
        document.createTextNode(' '),
        openButton,
        document.createTextNode(' '),
        exportButton,
        document.createTextNode(' '),
        deleteButton
      );
      backendResultNode.appendChild(row);
    }
  }

  function nextBackendRequestId() {
    backendRequestCounter += 1;
    return `${APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.requestIdPrefix}${backendRequestCounter}`;
  }

  async function executeBackendCommand(command, payload = {}) {
    const response = await backendRuntimeClient.execute({
      requestId: nextBackendRequestId(),
      module: APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.moduleIds.platform,
      command,
      payload
    });

    if (!response.ok) {
      logger.warn(
        APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.backend,
        APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendCommandFailed,
        response.error || null
      );
      setBackendResult(response);
      return null;
    }

    setBackendResult(response.result || {});
    return response.result || null;
  }

  async function openBackendProject(project) {
    const projectId = String(project?.id || '').trim();
    if (!projectId) {
      return;
    }

    const canContinue = await confirmSaveIfDirty();
    if (canContinue === APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.closeFlowDecisions.cancel) {
      return;
    }

    const result = await executeBackendCommand(
      APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.commands.openProject,
      { projectId }
    );

    if (!result?.snapshot) {
      return;
    }

    await tabs.closeAllTabs();
    logger.clear();
    await projectManager.openProjectSnapshot(result.snapshot);
    await tree.render();
  }

  async function exportBackendProject(project) {
    await runBackendProjectExport({
      project,
      exportCommandId: APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.commands.exportProject,
      executeBackendCommand,
      downloadBinary: (downloadUrl) => backendRuntimeClient.downloadBinary(downloadUrl),
      saveBinaryFileAsDialog: (payload) => fileSystem.saveBinaryFileAsDialog(payload),
      dialogs: APP_CONFIG.platform.app.dialogs,
      loggerWarn: (...args) => logger.warn(...args),
      loggerSource: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.backend,
      downloadFailedText: APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendExportDownloadFailed,
      setResult: setBackendResult
    });
  }

  async function refreshBackendProjects() {
    const result = await executeBackendCommand(APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.commands.listProjects);
    const projects = Array.isArray(result?.projects) ? result.projects : [];
    renderBackendProjects(projects);
  }

  async function deleteBackendProject(project) {
    await deleteBackendProjectFlow({
      project,
      confirmDelete: window.confirm,
      confirmPrefix: APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendDeleteConfirmPrefix,
      deleteCommandId: APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.commands.deleteProject,
      executeBackendCommand,
      closeDeletedProject: async (projectId) => closeDeletedBackendProjectIfOpened({
        projectId,
        projectManager,
        backendSource: APP_CONFIG.project.sources.backend,
        tabs,
        logger,
        tree
      }),
      refreshBackendProjects
    });
  }

  backendListButton?.addEventListener('click', () => {
    void refreshBackendProjects();
  });

  backendCreateButton?.addEventListener('click', () => {
    const name = String(backendCreateInput?.value || '').trim();
    void executeBackendCommand(
      APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.commands.createProject,
      { name }
    ).then((result) => {
      if (result?.project) {
        void refreshBackendProjects();
      }
    });
  });

  function getActiveParamsUndoRedoState() {
    const runtime = tabs.getActiveRuntime?.();
    if (!runtime?.supportsParamsUndoRedo?.()) {
      return {
        runtime: null,
        supported: false,
        isContextActive: false,
        canUndo: false,
        canRedo: false
      };
    }

    const state = runtime.getParamsUndoRedoState?.();
    const isContextActive = Boolean(
      state?.isContextActive
      ?? state?.isParamsUndoRedoContextActive
      ?? state?.isHotkeyContextActive
      ?? runtime?.isParamsUndoRedoContextActive?.()
    );

    return {
      runtime,
      supported: Boolean(state?.supported ?? true),
      isContextActive,
      canUndo: Boolean(state?.canUndo ?? runtime?.canUndoParams?.()),
      canRedo: Boolean(state?.canRedo ?? runtime?.canRedoParams?.())
    };
  }

  function updateParamsUndoRedoButtonsState() {
    if (!paramsUndoButton || !paramsRedoButton) {
      return;
    }

    const state = getActiveParamsUndoRedoState();

    paramsUndoButton.disabled = !state.supported || !state.isContextActive || !state.canUndo;
    paramsRedoButton.disabled = !state.supported || !state.isContextActive || !state.canRedo;
  }

  async function triggerParamsUndo() {
    const state = getActiveParamsUndoRedoState();
    if (!state.runtime || !state.supported || !state.isContextActive || !state.canUndo) {
      updateParamsUndoRedoButtonsState();
      return;
    }

    await state.runtime.undoParams?.();
    updateParamsUndoRedoButtonsState();
  }

  async function triggerParamsRedo() {
    const state = getActiveParamsUndoRedoState();
    if (!state.runtime || !state.supported || !state.isContextActive || !state.canRedo) {
      updateParamsUndoRedoButtonsState();
      return;
    }

    await state.runtime.redoParams?.();
    updateParamsUndoRedoButtonsState();
  }

  paramsUndoButton?.addEventListener('click', () => {
    void triggerParamsUndo();
  });

  paramsRedoButton?.addEventListener('click', () => {
    void triggerParamsRedo();
  });

  document.addEventListener('focusin', () => {
    updateParamsUndoRedoButtonsState();
  });
  document.addEventListener('pointerdown', () => {
    updateParamsUndoRedoButtonsState();
  }, true);
  updateParamsUndoRedoButtonsState();


  projectManager = createProjectManager({
    logger,
    fileSystem,
    moduleRegistry,
    onProjectLoaded: ({ projectRuntime }) => {
      window.MetaPlatformRuntime.activeProject = projectRuntime;
    },
    onProjectClosed: () => {
      window.MetaPlatformRuntime.activeProject = null;
    }
  });

  async function handleCreateComponentRequest(moduleId) {
    const module = moduleRegistry.getModule(moduleId);

    if (!module) {
      logger.warn(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.projectTree, 'Не найден модуль для создания компонента', { moduleId });
      return;
    }

    const defaultName = moduleId === APP_CONFIG.project.moduleIds.metagen
      ? projectManager.getNextMetaGenDefaultName()
      : module.getDefaultName?.() || APP_CONFIG.ui.text.untitled;

    await tabs.startTemporaryDocumentCreation({
      moduleId,
      defaultName,
      onCommit: async ({ moduleId: confirmedModuleId, confirmedName }) => {
        return projectManager.createDocument(confirmedModuleId, confirmedName);
      }
    });
  }

  async function handleDeleteComponentRequest(documentRecord) {
    const documentIdentity = getDocumentIdentityKey(documentRecord);
    await projectManager.deleteDocument(documentIdentity);
    await tabs.closeTab(documentIdentity, { skipProjectSync: true });
  }

  const tree = createProjectTree({
    logger,
    projectManager,
    tabs,
    onCreateComponentRequest: handleCreateComponentRequest,
    onDeleteComponentRequest: handleDeleteComponentRequest
  });

  async function saveProjectFlow({ forceSaveAs = false } = {}) {
    const project = projectManager.getCurrentProject();

    if (!project) {
      logger.warn(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.project, 'Нет открытого проекта для сохранения');
      return false;
    }

    const openDocuments = await tabs.collectOpenDocumentRecords();
    const isBackendSource = project.source === APP_CONFIG.project.sources.backend;

    if (isBackendSource && !forceSaveAs) {
      const payload = projectManager.buildBackendSavePayload(openDocuments);
      const result = await executeBackendCommand(
        APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.commands.saveAll,
        payload
      );

      if (!result) {
        return false;
      }

      projectManager.commitBackendSave(result?.project || null);
      await tree.render();
      logger.clear();
      return true;
    }

    if (isBackendSource && forceSaveAs) {
      const initialName = String(
        project.backendProject?.name
        || project.project?.name
        || APP_CONFIG.project.defaultProjectName
      ).trim() || APP_CONFIG.project.defaultProjectName;
      const newName = await showTextInputDialog({
        title: APP_CONFIG.platform.app.dialogs.saveProjectAsTitle,
        initialValue: initialName,
        confirmText: APP_CONFIG.ui.text.save,
        cancelText: APP_CONFIG.ui.text.cancel
      });

      if (!newName) {
        return false;
      }

      const payload = projectManager.buildBackendSaveAsPayload(newName, openDocuments);
      const result = await executeBackendCommand(
        APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.commands.saveProjectAs,
        payload
      );

      if (!result) {
        return false;
      }

      projectManager.commitBackendSaveAs(result?.project || null);
      await tree.render();
      logger.clear();
      return true;
    }

    if (project.isUnsaved || forceSaveAs) {
      const projectStem = String(project.project?.name || APP_CONFIG.project.defaultProjectName).trim() || APP_CONFIG.project.defaultProjectName;
      const suggestedPath = project.projectFilePath
        || buildProjectFilePath(project.rootPath || '.', `${projectStem}${APP_CONFIG.project.fileExtensions.default}`);
      const targetProjectFilePath = await fileSystem.saveProjectFileAsDialog(suggestedPath);

      if (!targetProjectFilePath) {
        return false;
      }

      const result = await projectManager.saveProjectAs(targetProjectFilePath, openDocuments);
      tabs.updateTabPaths(result?.pathMap);
      await tree.render();
      logger.clear();
      return true;
    }

    const result = await projectManager.saveProject(openDocuments);
    if (!result) { // Defensive guard for non-backend unsupported state.
      return false;
    }
    tabs.updateTabPaths(result?.pathMap);
    await tree.render();
    logger.clear();
    return true;
  }

  async function confirmSaveIfDirty() {
    if (!projectManager.hasDirtyProject()) {
      return APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.closeFlowDecisions.continue;
    }

    const decision = await showSaveChangesDialog({
      title: APP_CONFIG.ui.text.saveChangesTitle
    });

    if (decision === APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.dialogResults.cancel) {
      return APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.closeFlowDecisions.cancel;
    }

    if (decision === APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.dialogResults.discard) {
      return APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.closeFlowDecisions.continue;
    }

    const saved = await saveProjectFlow();
    return saved
      ? APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.closeFlowDecisions.continue
      : APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.closeFlowDecisions.cancel;
  }

  async function newProjectFlow() {
    const canContinue = await confirmSaveIfDirty();

    if (canContinue === APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.closeFlowDecisions.cancel) {
      return;
    }

    await tabs.closeAllTabs();
    logger.clear();
    await projectManager.createNewProject();
  }

  async function openProjectFlow() {
    const canContinue = await confirmSaveIfDirty();

    if (canContinue === APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.closeFlowDecisions.cancel) {
      return;
    }

    const selectedPath = await fileSystem.openProjectFileDialog();

    if (!selectedPath) {
      return;
    }

    await tabs.closeAllTabs();
    logger.clear();
    await projectManager.openProject(selectedPath);
  }

  async function closeProjectFlow() {
    if (!projectManager.getCurrentProject()) {
      return;
    }

    const canContinue = await confirmSaveIfDirty();

    if (canContinue === APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.closeFlowDecisions.cancel) {
      return;
    }

    await tabs.closeAllTabs();
    logger.clear();
    await projectManager.closeProject();
  }

  const appCloseCoordinator = createAppCloseCoordinator({
    confirmSaveIfDirty,
    requestAppQuit: () => fileSystem.requestAppQuit(),
    approveWindowClose: () => fileSystem.approveWindowClose(),
    cancelWindowClose: () => fileSystem.cancelWindowClose()
  });

  async function exitFlow() {
    await appCloseCoordinator.requestExit();
  }

  fileSystem.onWindowCloseRequested(async () => {
    try {
      await appCloseCoordinator.handleWindowCloseRequested();
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.windowClose, 'Ошибка обработки запроса закрытия окна', {
        message: error?.message || String(error)
      });

      try {
        await fileSystem.cancelWindowClose();
      } catch (cancelError) {
        logger.error(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.windowClose, 'Ошибка отмены закрытия окна', {
          message: cancelError?.message || String(cancelError)
        });
      }
    }
  });

  fileSystem.onMenuAction(async (action) => {
    try {
      const transitionResult = await tabs.finalizeActiveEditorContextBeforeTransition({
        reason: `${APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.transitionReasons.menuActionPrefix}${action}`,
        blockOnFailure: true
      });

      if (!transitionResult.continued) {
        logger.error(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.menu, 'Действие меню заблокировано: не удалось завершить редактирование перед сменой контекста', {
          action,
          outcome: transitionResult.outcome,
          reason: transitionResult.reason
        });
        return;
      }

      if (action === APP_CONFIG.platform.app.menu.actionIds.newProject) await newProjectFlow();
      if (action === APP_CONFIG.platform.app.menu.actionIds.openProject) await openProjectFlow();
      if (action === APP_CONFIG.platform.app.menu.actionIds.closeProject) await closeProjectFlow();
      if (action === APP_CONFIG.platform.app.menu.actionIds.save) await saveProjectFlow();
      if (action === APP_CONFIG.platform.app.menu.actionIds.saveAs) await saveProjectFlow({ forceSaveAs: true });
      if (action === APP_CONFIG.platform.app.menu.actionIds.exit) await exitFlow();
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.menu, 'Ошибка выполнения команды меню', {
        action,
        message: error?.message || String(error)
      });
    }
  });

  logger.info(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.platform, 'Инициализация MetaPlatform...');
  await tree.render();

  window.MetaPlatformRuntime = {
    logger,
    commandBus,
    moduleRegistry,
    projectManager,
    fileSystem,
    workbenchLayout,
    tabs,
    activeProject: projectManager.getCurrentProject()
  };
});


==================================================
FILE: renderer/core/commandBus.js
==================================================

import { APP_CONFIG } from '../../config/app-config.js';

const COMMAND_BUS_LOG_SOURCE = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.commandBus;
const COMMAND_BUS_MESSAGES = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.commandBusMessages;

export function createCommandBus({ logger }) {
  const handlers = new Map();

  function register(commandType, handler) {
    handlers.set(commandType, handler);
  }

  async function execute(command) {
    const type = command?.type;

    if (!type) {
      throw new Error(COMMAND_BUS_MESSAGES.commandTypeRequired);
    }

    const handler = handlers.get(type);

    if (!handler) {
      logger.warn(COMMAND_BUS_LOG_SOURCE, `${COMMAND_BUS_MESSAGES.missingHandlerPrefix}${type}`);
      return null;
    }

    logger.info(COMMAND_BUS_LOG_SOURCE, `${COMMAND_BUS_MESSAGES.executionPrefix}${type}`, command?.meta || null);

    try {
      const result = await handler(command);
      logger.info(COMMAND_BUS_LOG_SOURCE, `${COMMAND_BUS_MESSAGES.successPrefix}${type}`);
      return result;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error(COMMAND_BUS_LOG_SOURCE, `${COMMAND_BUS_MESSAGES.failurePrefix}${type}`, {
        message: error?.message || String(error)
      });
      throw error;
    }
  }

  return {
    register,
    execute
  };
}

import { APP_CONFIG } from '../../config/app-config.js';
import Split from 'split.js';

function getSplitSharedOptions() {
  return {
    elementStyle: (dimension, size, gutterSize) => ({
      'flex-basis': `calc(${size}% - ${gutterSize}px)`
    }),
    gutterStyle: (dimension, gutterSize) => ({
      'flex-basis': `${gutterSize}px`
    })
  };
}

export function initWorkbenchLayout() {
  const horizontalSplit = Split([`#${APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.projectTreeColumnId}`, `#${APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.workbenchRightColumnId}`], {
    ...APP_CONFIG.ui.layout.split.horizontal,
    ...getSplitSharedOptions()
  });

  const verticalSplit = Split([`#${APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.editorHostContainerId}`, `#${APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.bottomPanelId}`], {
    ...APP_CONFIG.ui.layout.split.vertical,
    ...getSplitSharedOptions()
  });

  return {
    dispose() {
      horizontalSplit?.destroy?.();
      verticalSplit?.destroy?.();
    }
  };
}


==================================================
FILE: renderer/core/logger.js
==================================================

import { APP_CONFIG } from '../../config/app-config.js';
import { normalizeLogDetails } from './loggerShared.js';

const LOGGER_LEVELS = APP_CONFIG.logger.levels;
const LOGGER_LEVEL_NAMES = APP_CONFIG.logger.levelNames;

function resolveConfigLevel() {
  return APP_CONFIG.platform?.logging?.level || LOGGER_LEVEL_NAMES.info;
}

function shouldWrite(level) {
  const targetLevel = resolveConfigLevel();
  const targetPriority = LOGGER_LEVELS[targetLevel] ?? LOGGER_LEVELS.info;
  const entryPriority = LOGGER_LEVELS[level] ?? LOGGER_LEVELS.info;
  return entryPriority >= targetPriority && targetPriority < LOGGER_LEVELS.none;
}

export function createCoreLogger({ sinks = [] } = {}) {
  function write(level, source, message, details = null) {
    if (!shouldWrite(level)) {
      return;
    }

    const ts = new Date().toLocaleTimeString(APP_CONFIG.platform.locale);
    const line = `[${ts}] [${source}] ${level.toUpperCase()} ${message}`;
    const detailsText = details != null ? normalizeLogDetails(details) : '';
    const entry = { level, source, message, line, details, detailsText, ts };

    sinks.forEach((sink) => sink?.write?.(entry));
  }

  function clear() {
    sinks.forEach((sink) => sink?.clear?.());
  }

  return {
    debug: (source, message, details = null) => write(LOGGER_LEVEL_NAMES.debug, source, message, details),
    info: (source, message, details = null) => write(LOGGER_LEVEL_NAMES.info, source, message, details),
    warn: (source, message, details = null) => write(LOGGER_LEVEL_NAMES.warn, source, message, details),
    error: (source, message, details = null) => write(LOGGER_LEVEL_NAMES.error, source, message, details),
    clear
  };
}

export { shouldWrite };


==================================================
FILE: renderer/core/loggerShared.js
==================================================

import { LOGGER_CONFIG } from '../../config/logger-config.js';

const LOGGER_PRETTY_PRINT_INDENT = LOGGER_CONFIG.format.prettyPrintIndent;

export function normalizeLogDetails(details) {
  if (details == null) {
    return '';
  }

  if (typeof details === 'string') {
    return details;
  }

  try {
    return JSON.stringify(details, null, LOGGER_PRETTY_PRINT_INDENT);
  } catch {
    return String(details);
  }
}


==================================================
FILE: renderer/core/moduleRegistry.js
==================================================

import { APP_CONFIG } from '../../config/app-config.js';

const MODULE_REGISTRY_LOG_SOURCE = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.moduleRegistry;

export function createModuleRegistry({ logger }) {
  const modulesById = new Map();
  const documentKindToModuleId = new Map();

  function registerModule(module) {
    if (!module?.id) {
      throw new Error('Module id is required');
    }

    modulesById.set(module.id, module);

    for (const kind of module.documentKinds || []) {
      documentKindToModuleId.set(kind, module.id);
    }

    logger.info(MODULE_REGISTRY_LOG_SOURCE, 'Модуль зарегистрирован', {
      id: module.id,
      name: module.name,
      documentKinds: module.documentKinds || []
    });
  }

  function getModule(moduleId) {
    return modulesById.get(moduleId) || null;
  }

  function getAllModules() {
    return [...modulesById.values()];
  }

  function findModuleByDocumentKind(kind) {
    const moduleId = documentKindToModuleId.get(kind);
    return moduleId ? getModule(moduleId) : null;
  }

  return {
    registerModule,
    getModule,
    getAllModules,
    findModuleByDocumentKind
  };
}
