FILE: renderer/modules/metagen/metagenModule.js
==================================================

import { APP_CONFIG } from '../../../config/app-config.js';
import { createMetaGenDocument } from './metagenDocumentFactory.js';
import { validateMetaGenDocument } from './metagenSchema.js';
import { createMetaGenEditor } from '../../editors/metagen/createMetaGenEditor.js';
import { slugifyDocumentName } from '../../runtime/naming.js';
import { METAGEN_CONFIG } from './metagenConfig.js';

export function createMetaGenModule({ logger }) {
  return {
    id: METAGEN_CONFIG.moduleId,
    name: METAGEN_CONFIG.moduleName,
    documentKinds: [METAGEN_CONFIG.documentKind],

    getDefaultName() {
      return METAGEN_CONFIG.defaults.newDocumentName;
    },

    createDefaultDocument({ name }) {
      return createMetaGenDocument({ name });
    },

    getFileName(document) {
      return `${slugifyDocumentName(document?.component?.name || METAGEN_CONFIG.defaults.newDocumentName)}${APP_CONFIG.project.fileExtensions.default}`;
    },

    validate(document) {
      return validateMetaGenDocument(document);
    },

    async openDocument({ documentRecord, mountElement, onDirty }) {
      return createMetaGenEditor({
        documentRecord,
        mountElement,
        logger,
        onDirty,
        onSave: async (nextRecord) => {
          const validation = validateMetaGenDocument(nextRecord.document);

          if (!validation.isValid) {
            logger.warn(METAGEN_CONFIG.moduleId, 'Документ MetaGen не прошёл валидацию', validation.errors);
            throw new Error(validation.errors.join('; '));
          }

          return true;
        }
      });
    }
  };
}


==================================================
FILE: renderer/modules/metagen/metagenSchema.js
==================================================

import { METAGEN_CONFIG } from './metagenConfig.js';

export function validateMetaGenDocument(document) {
  const errors = [];

  if (!document || document.kind !== METAGEN_CONFIG.documentKind) {
    errors.push(`kind должен быть ${METAGEN_CONFIG.documentKind}`);
  }

  if (!document?.component?.name) {
    errors.push('component.name обязателен');
  }

  const instances = document?.instances;
  const hasInstancesObject = instances && typeof instances === 'object' && !Array.isArray(instances);

  if (instances != null && !hasInstancesObject) {
    errors.push('instances должен быть объектом');
  }

  if (hasInstancesObject && instances.format != null && instances.format !== METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.list) {
    errors.push(`instances.format должен быть ${METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.list}`);
  }

  if (hasInstancesObject && instances.rows != null && !Array.isArray(instances.rows)) {
    errors.push('instances.rows должен быть массивом');
  }

  return {
    isValid: errors.length === 0,
    errors
  };
}


==================================================
FILE: renderer/modules/metagen/metagenParamsContract.js
==================================================

import { METAGEN_CONFIG } from './metagenConfig.js';

function normalizeRowLike(value) {
  if (Array.isArray(value)) {
    return value.map((cell) => cell ?? '');
  }

  if (value == null) {
    return [];
  }

  return [value];
}

export function normalizeMetaGenParamsDocument(paramsDocument) {
  if (Array.isArray(paramsDocument)) {
    const rows = paramsDocument.map((row) => normalizeRowLike(row));

    return {
      format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.headerPlusRows,
      header: rows[0] || [],
      rows: rows.slice(1)
    };
  }

  const header = normalizeRowLike(paramsDocument?.header);
  const rows = Array.isArray(paramsDocument?.rows)
    ? paramsDocument.rows.map((row) => normalizeRowLike(row))
    : [];

  return {
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.headerPlusRows,
    header,
    rows
  };
}

export function getMetaGenParamsRequiredDimensions(paramsDocument, tableConfig, options = {}) {
  const normalized = normalizeMetaGenParamsDocument(paramsDocument);
  const rows = [normalized.header, ...normalized.rows];
  // Runtime sheet semantics: always open at max(bootstrap seed, persisted payload shape).
  // Persisted payload itself stays compact via extract/save path.
  const payloadRows = rows.length || 1;
  const requiredRows = Math.max(Number(tableConfig?.rows) || 1, payloadRows);
  const widestRow = rows.reduce((maxValue, row) => Math.max(maxValue, Array.isArray(row) ? row.length : 0), 0);
  const payloadColumns = widestRow || 1;
  const requiredColumns = Math.max(Number(tableConfig?.defaultColumns) || 1, payloadColumns);

  return {
    rowCount: requiredRows,
    columnCount: requiredColumns,
    normalized
  };
}


==================================================
FILE: renderer/modules/metagen/metagenDataContract.js
==================================================

import { METAGEN_CONFIG } from './metagenConfig.js';

function normalizeRowLike(value) {
  if (Array.isArray(value)) {
    return value.map((cell) => cell ?? '');
  }

  if (value == null) {
    return [];
  }

  return [value];
}

export function normalizeMetaGenDataDocument(dataDocument, tableConfig = {}) {
  const fallbackColumns = Array.isArray(tableConfig?.headers) ? [...tableConfig.headers] : [];

  const columns = Array.isArray(dataDocument?.columns) && dataDocument.columns.length > 0
    ? [...dataDocument.columns]
    : fallbackColumns;

  const rows = Array.isArray(dataDocument?.rows)
    ? dataDocument.rows.map((row) => normalizeRowLike(row))
    : [];

  return {
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.table,
    columns,
    rows
  };
}


export function hasPersistedMetaGenDataShape(dataDocument) {
  if (!dataDocument || typeof dataDocument !== 'object') {
    return false;
  }

  const hasRows = Array.isArray(dataDocument.rows) && dataDocument.rows.length > 0;
  const hasColumns = Array.isArray(dataDocument.columns) && dataDocument.columns.length > 0;

  return hasRows || hasColumns;
}

export function getMetaGenDataRequiredDimensions(dataDocument, tableConfig = {}, options = {}) {
  const normalized = normalizeMetaGenDataDocument(dataDocument, tableConfig);
  const bootstrapRows = Math.max(1, Number(tableConfig?.rows) || 1);
  const bootstrapColumns = Math.max(1, Array.isArray(tableConfig?.headers) ? tableConfig.headers.length : 0);

  const widestRow = normalized.rows.reduce(
    (maxValue, row) => Math.max(maxValue, Array.isArray(row) ? row.length : 0),
    0
  );

  // Runtime sheet semantics: always open at max(bootstrap seed, persisted payload shape).
  // Persisted payload itself stays compact via extract/save path.
  const payloadRows = normalized.rows.length || 1;
  const payloadColumns = Math.max(normalized.columns.length || 0, widestRow || 0, 1);

  return {
    rowCount: Math.max(bootstrapRows, payloadRows),
    columnCount: Math.max(bootstrapColumns, payloadColumns),
    normalized
  };
}


==================================================
FILE: renderer/modules/metagen/metagenInstancesContract.js
==================================================

import { METAGEN_CONFIG } from './metagenConfig.js';

function normalizeRowLike(value) {
  if (Array.isArray(value)) {
    return value.map((cell) => cell ?? '');
  }

  if (value == null) {
    return [];
  }

  return [value];
}

function normalizeInstancesRow(row, fixedColumnCount) {
  const normalizedRow = normalizeRowLike(row).slice(0, fixedColumnCount);

  while (normalizedRow.length < fixedColumnCount) {
    normalizedRow.push('');
  }

  return normalizedRow;
}

export function normalizeMetaGenInstancesDocument(instancesDocument, tableConfig = {}) {
  const fixedColumnCount = Math.max(1, Number(tableConfig?.fixedColumnCount) || 1);
  const rows = Array.isArray(instancesDocument?.rows)
    ? instancesDocument.rows.map((row) => normalizeInstancesRow(row, fixedColumnCount))
    : [];

  return {
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.list,
    rows
  };
}

export function hasPersistedMetaGenInstancesShape(instancesDocument) {
  if (!instancesDocument || typeof instancesDocument !== 'object') {
    return false;
  }

  return Array.isArray(instancesDocument.rows) && instancesDocument.rows.length > 0;
}

export function getMetaGenInstancesRequiredDimensions(instancesDocument, tableConfig = {}) {
  const normalized = normalizeMetaGenInstancesDocument(instancesDocument, tableConfig);
  const bootstrapRows = Math.max(1, Number(tableConfig?.rows) || 1);
  const fixedColumnCount = Math.max(1, Number(tableConfig?.fixedColumnCount) || 1);
  const payloadRows = normalized.rows.length || 1;

  return {
    rowCount: Math.max(bootstrapRows, payloadRows),
    columnCount: fixedColumnCount,
    normalized
  };
}


==================================================
FILE: renderer/modules/metagen/tables/createMetaGenDataSheet.js
==================================================

import { createMetaGenSimpleSheet } from './createMetaGenSimpleSheet.js';
import { METAGEN_CONFIG } from '../metagenConfig.js';
import { readTableDocument, trimTrailingEmptyRows } from './sheetSnapshot.js';
import {
  getMetaGenDataRequiredDimensions,
  hasPersistedMetaGenDataShape,
  normalizeMetaGenDataDocument
} from '../metagenDataContract.js';


function buildHiddenMenuConfig(commands) {
  return Object.fromEntries(commands.map((command) => [command, { hidden: true }]));
}

function sleep(delayMs) {
  return new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, delayMs));
}

async function applyHeaderConfig({ sheet, headers, headerConfig, retryConfig, logger, source, logMessages }) {
  if (!sheet || typeof sheet.customizeColumnHeader !== 'function') {
    logger.warn(source, logMessages.headerMethodUnavailable);
    return false;
  }

  const applyConfig = () => {
    if (!headerConfig || headerConfig.mode === 'default') {
      sheet.customizeColumnHeader({ columnsCfg: {} });
      logger.info(source, logMessages.defaultHeadersApplied);
      return;
    }

    const columnsCfg = headers.reduce((accumulator, text, index) => {
      if (text != null && text !== '') {
        accumulator[index] = text;
      }
      return accumulator;
    }, {});

    sheet.customizeColumnHeader({
      columnsCfg,
      headerStyle: headerConfig.headerStyle || {}
    });

    logger.info(source, logMessages.customHeadersApplied);
  };

  for (let attemptIndex = 0; attemptIndex < retryConfig.retryCount; attemptIndex += 1) {
    try {
      applyConfig();
      return true;
    } catch (error) {
      const message = error?.message || String(error);

      if (!message.includes('Render Unit with unitId')) {
        throw error;
      }

      logger.warn(
        source,
        `${logMessages.headerApplyRetryPrefix} (${attemptIndex + 1}/${retryConfig.retryCount})`
      );
      await sleep(retryConfig.retryDelayMs);
    }
  }

  logger.warn(source, logMessages.headerApplyFailed);
  return false;
}

async function applyDataSheetPermissions({ univerAPI, sheet, permissions, logger, source, logMessages }) {
  const worksheetPermission = sheet.getWorksheetPermission();

  await worksheetPermission.protect();
  await worksheetPermission.setPoint(
    univerAPI.Enum.WorksheetPermissionPoint.SetCellValue,
    permissions.allowSetCellValue
  );
  await worksheetPermission.setPoint(
    univerAPI.Enum.WorksheetPermissionPoint.InsertColumn,
    permissions.allowInsertColumn
  );
  await worksheetPermission.setPoint(
    univerAPI.Enum.WorksheetPermissionPoint.DeleteColumn,
    permissions.allowDeleteColumn
  );

  logger.info(source, logMessages.dataColumnsProtectionApplied);
}

function applyCheckboxValidation({ univerAPI, sheet, rowCount, headers, checkboxColumns, logger, source, logMessages }) {
  try {
    checkboxColumns
      .map((columnName) => headers.indexOf(columnName))
      .filter((index) => index !== -1)
      .forEach((columnIndex) => {
        const range = sheet.getRange(0, columnIndex, rowCount, 1);
        const checkboxRule = univerAPI.newDataValidation().requireCheckbox().build();
        range.setDataValidation(checkboxRule);
      });

    logger.info(source, logMessages.checkboxColumnsConfigured);
  } catch (error) {
    logger.warn(source, logMessages.checkboxColumnsFailed, error);
  }
}


function resolveSheetDimension(sheet, methodNames, fallback) {
  for (const methodName of methodNames) {
    const method = sheet?.[methodName];

    if (typeof method !== 'function') {
      continue;
    }

    const value = Number(method.call(sheet));

    if (Number.isFinite(value) && value > 0) {
      return Math.floor(value);
    }
  }

  return Math.max(1, Number(fallback) || 1);
}

function writeDataDocumentToSheet(sheet, dataDocument, columnCount) {
  const normalized = normalizeMetaGenDataDocument(dataDocument);

  normalized.rows.forEach((rowValues, rowIndex) => {
    if (!Array.isArray(rowValues) || rowValues.length === 0) {
      return;
    }

    const limited = rowValues.slice(0, columnCount);
    sheet.getRange(rowIndex, 0, 1, limited.length).setValues([limited]);
  });
}

function extractRows(sheet, tableConfig) {
  const maxRows = resolveSheetDimension(sheet, ['getRowCount', 'getMaxRows', 'getSheetRowCount'], 1);
  const maxColumns = resolveSheetDimension(sheet, ['getColumnCount', 'getMaxColumns', 'getSheetColumnCount'], 1);

  return trimTrailingEmptyRows(readTableDocument(sheet, {
    maxRows,
    maxColumns,
    columns: []
  }).rows);
}

export function extractDataDocumentValue(sheet, tableConfig) {
  return {
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.table,
    columns: [...tableConfig.headers],
    rows: extractRows(sheet, tableConfig)
  };
}

export async function createMetaGenDataSheet({
  container,
  locale,
  logger,
  source,
  workbookId,
  workbookName,
  sheetId,
  sheetName,
  dataValidationPreset,
  tableConfig,
  hiddenMenuCommands,
  logMessages,
  dataDocument
}) {
  const normalizedDataDocument = normalizeMetaGenDataDocument(dataDocument, tableConfig);
  const initialDimensions = getMetaGenDataRequiredDimensions(normalizedDataDocument, tableConfig, {
    bootstrapMode: hasPersistedMetaGenDataShape(dataDocument)
      ? METAGEN_CONFIG.bootstrapModes.hydrate
      : METAGEN_CONFIG.bootstrapModes.seed
  });

  const sheetRuntime = createMetaGenSimpleSheet({
    container,
    locale,
    menu: buildHiddenMenuConfig(hiddenMenuCommands),
    workbookId,
    workbookName,
    sheetId,
    sheetName,
    rowCount: initialDimensions.rowCount,
    columnCount: initialDimensions.columnCount,
    logger,
    source,
    logMessages,
    extraPresets: typeof dataValidationPreset === 'function' ? [dataValidationPreset()] : []
  });

  if (!sheetRuntime) {
    return null;
  }

  writeDataDocumentToSheet(sheetRuntime.sheet, initialDimensions.normalized, initialDimensions.columnCount);

  await applyDataSheetPermissions({
    univerAPI: sheetRuntime.univerAPI,
    sheet: sheetRuntime.sheet,
    permissions: tableConfig.permissions,
    logger,
    source,
    logMessages
  });

  applyCheckboxValidation({
    univerAPI: sheetRuntime.univerAPI,
    sheet: sheetRuntime.sheet,
    rowCount: initialDimensions.rowCount,
    headers: tableConfig.headers,
    checkboxColumns: tableConfig.checkboxColumns,
    logger,
    source,
    logMessages
  });

  await applyHeaderConfig({
    sheet: sheetRuntime.sheet,
    headers: tableConfig.headers,
    headerConfig: tableConfig.headerConfig,
    retryConfig: tableConfig.headerApply,
    logger,
    source,
    logMessages
  });

  return {
    ...sheetRuntime,
    extractDocumentValue() {
      return extractDataDocumentValue(sheetRuntime.sheet, tableConfig);
    }
  };
}

import { createMetaGenSimpleSheet } from './createMetaGenSimpleSheet.js';
import { METAGEN_CONFIG } from '../metagenConfig.js';
import { readTableDocument, trimTrailingEmptyRows } from './sheetSnapshot.js';
import {
  getMetaGenInstancesRequiredDimensions,
  normalizeMetaGenInstancesDocument
} from '../metagenInstancesContract.js';

function buildHiddenMenuConfig(commands) {
  return Object.fromEntries(commands.map((command) => [command, { hidden: true }]));
}

function sleep(delayMs) {
  return new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, delayMs));
}

async function applyHeaderConfig({ sheet, headers, headerConfig, retryConfig, logger, source, logMessages }) {
  if (!sheet || typeof sheet.customizeColumnHeader !== 'function') {
    logger.warn(source, logMessages.headerMethodUnavailable);
    return false;
  }

  const applyConfig = () => {
    if (!headerConfig || headerConfig.mode === 'default') {
      sheet.customizeColumnHeader({ columnsCfg: {} });
      logger.info(source, logMessages.defaultHeadersApplied);
      return;
    }

    const columnsCfg = headers.reduce((accumulator, text, index) => {
      if (text != null && text !== '') {
        accumulator[index] = text;
      }
      return accumulator;
    }, {});

    sheet.customizeColumnHeader({
      columnsCfg,
      headerStyle: headerConfig.headerStyle || {}
    });

    logger.info(source, logMessages.customHeadersApplied);
  };

  for (let attemptIndex = 0; attemptIndex < retryConfig.retryCount; attemptIndex += 1) {
    try {
      applyConfig();
      return true;
    } catch (error) {
      const message = error?.message || String(error);

      if (!message.includes('Render Unit with unitId')) {
        throw error;
      }

      logger.warn(
        source,
        `${logMessages.headerApplyRetryPrefix} (${attemptIndex + 1}/${retryConfig.retryCount})`
      );
      await sleep(retryConfig.retryDelayMs);
    }
  }

  logger.warn(source, logMessages.headerApplyFailed);
  return false;
}

async function applyInstancesSheetPermissions({ univerAPI, sheet, permissions, logger, source, logMessages }) {
  const worksheetPermission = sheet.getWorksheetPermission();

  await worksheetPermission.protect();
  await worksheetPermission.setPoint(
    univerAPI.Enum.WorksheetPermissionPoint.SetCellValue,
    permissions.allowSetCellValue
  );
  await worksheetPermission.setPoint(
    univerAPI.Enum.WorksheetPermissionPoint.InsertColumn,
    permissions.allowInsertColumn
  );
  await worksheetPermission.setPoint(
    univerAPI.Enum.WorksheetPermissionPoint.DeleteColumn,
    permissions.allowDeleteColumn
  );

  logger.info(
    source,
    logMessages.instancesColumnsProtectionApplied || logMessages.dataColumnsProtectionApplied
  );
}

function resolveSheetDimension(sheet, methodNames, fallback) {
  for (const methodName of methodNames) {
    const method = sheet?.[methodName];

    if (typeof method !== 'function') {
      continue;
    }

    const value = Number(method.call(sheet));

    if (Number.isFinite(value) && value > 0) {
      return Math.floor(value);
    }
  }

  return Math.max(1, Number(fallback) || 1);
}

function writeInstancesDocumentToSheet(sheet, instancesDocument, columnCount) {
  const normalized = normalizeMetaGenInstancesDocument(instancesDocument, {
    fixedColumnCount: columnCount
  });

  normalized.rows.forEach((rowValues, rowIndex) => {
    if (!Array.isArray(rowValues) || rowValues.length === 0) {
      return;
    }

    const limited = rowValues.slice(0, columnCount);
    sheet.getRange(rowIndex, 0, 1, limited.length).setValues([limited]);
  });
}

function extractRows(sheet, tableConfig) {
  const maxRows = resolveSheetDimension(sheet, ['getRowCount', 'getMaxRows', 'getSheetRowCount'], 1);

  const rows = trimTrailingEmptyRows(readTableDocument(sheet, {
    maxRows,
    maxColumns: tableConfig.fixedColumnCount,
    columns: []
  }).rows);

  return rows.map((row) => normalizeMetaGenInstancesDocument({ rows: [row] }, tableConfig).rows[0]);
}

export function extractInstancesDocumentValue(sheet, tableConfig) {
  return {
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.list,
    rows: extractRows(sheet, tableConfig)
  };
}

export async function createMetaGenInstancesSheet({
  container,
  locale,
  logger,
  source,
  workbookId,
  workbookName,
  sheetId,
  sheetName,
  tableConfig,
  hiddenMenuCommands,
  logMessages,
  instancesDocument
}) {
  const normalizedInstancesDocument = normalizeMetaGenInstancesDocument(instancesDocument, tableConfig);
  const initialDimensions = getMetaGenInstancesRequiredDimensions(normalizedInstancesDocument, tableConfig);

  const sheetRuntime = createMetaGenSimpleSheet({
    container,
    locale,
    menu: buildHiddenMenuConfig(hiddenMenuCommands),
    workbookId,
    workbookName,
    sheetId,
    sheetName,
    rowCount: initialDimensions.rowCount,
    columnCount: tableConfig.fixedColumnCount,
    logger,
    source,
    logMessages
  });

  if (!sheetRuntime) {
    return null;
  }

  writeInstancesDocumentToSheet(sheetRuntime.sheet, initialDimensions.normalized, tableConfig.fixedColumnCount);

  await applyInstancesSheetPermissions({
    univerAPI: sheetRuntime.univerAPI,
    sheet: sheetRuntime.sheet,
    permissions: tableConfig.permissions,
    logger,
    source,
    logMessages
  });

  await applyHeaderConfig({
    sheet: sheetRuntime.sheet,
    headers: tableConfig.headers,
    headerConfig: tableConfig.headerConfig,
    retryConfig: tableConfig.headerApply,
    logger,
    source,
    logMessages
  });

  return {
    ...sheetRuntime,
    extractDocumentValue() {
      return extractInstancesDocumentValue(sheetRuntime.sheet, tableConfig);
    }
  };
}


==================================================
FILE: renderer/modules/metagen/tables/createMetaGenParamsSheet.js
==================================================

import { createMetaGenSimpleSheet } from './createMetaGenSimpleSheet.js';
import { METAGEN_CONFIG } from '../metagenConfig.js';
import { createMetaGenParamsTableAutoStyle } from './metaGenParamsTableAutoStyle.js';
import {
  getMetaGenParamsRequiredDimensions,
  normalizeMetaGenParamsDocument
} from '../metagenParamsContract.js';
import {
  readHeaderPlusRowsDocument
} from './sheetSnapshot.js';


function buildHiddenMenuConfig(commands = []) {
  return Object.fromEntries(commands.map((command) => [command, { hidden: true }]));
}

function hasPersistedParamsShape(paramsDocument) {
  if (!paramsDocument || !Array.isArray(paramsDocument.rows) || !Array.isArray(paramsDocument.header)) {
    return false;
  }

  return paramsDocument.header.length > 0 || paramsDocument.rows.length > 0;
}


function writeParamsDocumentToSheet(sheet, paramsDocument, columnCount) {
  const normalized = normalizeMetaGenParamsDocument(paramsDocument);
  const rows = [normalized.header, ...normalized.rows];

  rows.forEach((rowValues, rowIndex) => {
    if (!Array.isArray(rowValues) || rowValues.length === 0) {
      return;
    }

    const limited = rowValues.slice(0, columnCount);
    sheet.getRange(rowIndex, 0, 1, limited.length).setValues([limited]);
  });
}

function createEmptyRows(rowCount, columnCount) {
  return Array.from({ length: rowCount }, () => Array.from({ length: columnCount }, () => ''));
}

function canAccessRange(sheet, rowCount, columnCount) {
  try {
    sheet.getRange(0, 0, Math.max(1, rowCount), Math.max(1, columnCount));
    return true;
  } catch {
    return false;
  }
}

function resolveSheetDimension(sheet, methodNames, fallback) {
  for (const methodName of methodNames) {
    const method = sheet?.[methodName];

    if (typeof method !== 'function') {
      continue;
    }

    const value = Number(method.call(sheet));

    if (Number.isFinite(value) && value > 0) {
      return Math.floor(value);
    }
  }

  return Math.max(1, Number(fallback) || 1);
}

export function extractParamsDocumentValue(sheet, tableConfig) {
  const maxRows = resolveSheetDimension(sheet, ['getRowCount', 'getMaxRows', 'getSheetRowCount'], 1);
  const maxColumns = resolveSheetDimension(sheet, ['getColumnCount', 'getMaxColumns', 'getSheetColumnCount'], 1);

  return readHeaderPlusRowsDocument(sheet, {
    maxRows,
    maxColumns
  });
}

export function applyParamsDocumentValue(sheet, tableConfig, paramsDocument) {
  const dimensions = getMetaGenParamsRequiredDimensions(paramsDocument, tableConfig, {
    bootstrapMode: METAGEN_CONFIG.bootstrapModes.hydrate
  });
  const nextNormalized = dimensions.normalized;
  const actualRows = resolveSheetDimension(sheet, ['getRowCount', 'getMaxRows', 'getSheetRowCount'], 1);
  const actualColumns = resolveSheetDimension(sheet, ['getColumnCount', 'getMaxColumns', 'getSheetColumnCount'], 1);
  const targetClearRows = Math.max(actualRows, dimensions.rowCount);
  const targetClearColumns = Math.max(actualColumns, dimensions.columnCount);
  const clearRows = canAccessRange(sheet, targetClearRows, targetClearColumns) ? targetClearRows : actualRows;
  const clearColumns = canAccessRange(sheet, clearRows, targetClearColumns) ? targetClearColumns : actualColumns;

  sheet.getRange(0, 0, clearRows, clearColumns).setValues(createEmptyRows(clearRows, clearColumns));

  const sourceRows = [nextNormalized.header, ...nextNormalized.rows];
  sourceRows.forEach((rowValues, rowIndex) => {
    if (!Array.isArray(rowValues) || rowValues.length === 0) {
      return;
    }

    if (rowIndex >= clearRows) {
      return;
    }

    const limitedRowValues = rowValues.slice(0, clearColumns);

    if (limitedRowValues.length === 0) {
      return;
    }

    sheet.getRange(rowIndex, 0, 1, limitedRowValues.length).setValues([limitedRowValues]);
  });

  return nextNormalized;
}

export function createMetaGenParamsSheet({
  container,
  locale,
  logger,
  source,
  autoStyleSource,
  workbookId,
  workbookName,
  sheetId,
  sheetName,
  tableConfig,
  hiddenMenuCommands,
  logMessages,
  paramsDocument
}) {
  const normalizedParamsDocument = normalizeMetaGenParamsDocument(paramsDocument);
  const initialDimensions = getMetaGenParamsRequiredDimensions(normalizedParamsDocument, tableConfig, {
    bootstrapMode: hasPersistedParamsShape(normalizedParamsDocument)
      ? METAGEN_CONFIG.bootstrapModes.hydrate
      : METAGEN_CONFIG.bootstrapModes.seed
  });

  const sheetRuntime = createMetaGenSimpleSheet({
    container,
    locale,
    menu: buildHiddenMenuConfig(hiddenMenuCommands),
    workbookId,
    workbookName,
    sheetId,
    sheetName,
    rowCount: initialDimensions.rowCount,
    columnCount: initialDimensions.columnCount,
    logger,
    source,
    logMessages
  });

  if (!sheetRuntime) {
    return null;
  }

  writeParamsDocumentToSheet(sheetRuntime.sheet, initialDimensions.normalized, initialDimensions.columnCount);

  const autoStyleController = createMetaGenParamsTableAutoStyle({
    univerAPI: sheetRuntime.univerAPI,
    workbook: sheetRuntime.workbook,
    sheet: sheetRuntime.sheet,
    logger,
    source: autoStyleSource,
    logMessages,
    rowCount: initialDimensions.rowCount,
    columnCount: initialDimensions.columnCount,
    autoStyleConfig: tableConfig.autoStyle
  });

  return {
    ...sheetRuntime,
    ...autoStyleController,
    extractDocumentValue() {
      return extractParamsDocumentValue(sheetRuntime.sheet, tableConfig);
    },
    applyDocumentValue(nextDocumentValue, options = {}) {
      const nextNormalized = applyParamsDocumentValue(sheetRuntime.sheet, tableConfig, nextDocumentValue);

      if (options.refreshAutoStyle !== false) {
        autoStyleController?.refreshAll?.();
      }

      return nextNormalized;
    },
    refreshAutoStyle() {
      autoStyleController?.refreshAll?.();
    },
    beginReplayAutoStyleSuppression() {
      autoStyleController?.beginReplaySuppression?.();
    },
    endReplayAutoStyleSuppression() {
      autoStyleController?.endReplaySuppression?.();
    },
    refreshReplayAutoStyleBounds(bounds, options = {}) {
      autoStyleController?.refreshReplayBounds?.(bounds, options);
    },
    dispose() {
      autoStyleController?.dispose?.();
      sheetRuntime?.dispose?.();
    }
  };
}

import { createUniver, LocaleType } from '@univerjs/presets';
import { UniverSheetsCorePreset } from '@univerjs/preset-sheets-core';

export function createMetaGenSimpleSheet({
  container,
  locale,
  menu,
  toolbar = true,
  contextMenu = true,
  workbookId,
  workbookName,
  sheetId,
  sheetName,
  rowCount,
  columnCount,
  logger,
  source,
  logMessages,
  extraPresets = []
}) {
  try {
    const { univerAPI } = createUniver({
      locale: LocaleType.RU_RU,
      locales: {
        [LocaleType.RU_RU]: locale
      },
      presets: [
        UniverSheetsCorePreset({
          container,
          header: true,
          toolbar,
          contextMenu,
          footer: false,
          sheets: {
            protectedRangeShadow: false
          },
          ...(menu ? { menu } : {})
        }),
        ...extraPresets
      ]
    });

    const workbook = univerAPI.createWorkbook({
      id: workbookId,
      name: workbookName,
      sheetOrder: [sheetId],
      sheets: {
        [sheetId]: {
          id: sheetId,
          name: sheetName,
          rowCount,
          columnCount
        }
      }
    });

    const sheet = workbook.getActiveSheet();

    logger.info(source, logMessages.tableCreated, {
      workbookId,
      sheetId,
      sheetName
    });

    return {
      univerAPI,
      workbook,
      sheet,
      dispose() {
        if (typeof univerAPI.dispose === 'function') {
          univerAPI.dispose();
        }
      }
    };
  } catch (error) {
    logger.error(source, logMessages.tableCreateFailed, error);
    return null;
  }
}


==================================================
FILE: renderer/modules/metagen/tables/finalizeActiveTableEditing.js
==================================================

export const TABLE_EDIT_FINALIZE_RESULT = {
  COMMITTED: 'committed',
  CANCELLED: 'cancelled',
  NO_OP: 'no-op',
  FAILED: 'failed'
};

export async function finalizeActiveTableEditing({ tableRuntime, logger, source }) {
  if (!tableRuntime || typeof tableRuntime.isCellEditing !== 'function') {
    return TABLE_EDIT_FINALIZE_RESULT.NO_OP;
  }

  if (!tableRuntime.isCellEditing()) {
    return TABLE_EDIT_FINALIZE_RESULT.NO_OP;
  }

  if (typeof tableRuntime.endEditingAsync === 'function') {
    try {
      const committed = await tableRuntime.endEditingAsync(true);

      if (committed) {
        return TABLE_EDIT_FINALIZE_RESULT.COMMITTED;
      }

      if (typeof tableRuntime.abortEditingAsync === 'function') {
        const cancelled = await tableRuntime.abortEditingAsync();
        return cancelled ? TABLE_EDIT_FINALIZE_RESULT.CANCELLED : TABLE_EDIT_FINALIZE_RESULT.FAILED;
      }

      return TABLE_EDIT_FINALIZE_RESULT.FAILED;
    } catch (error) {
      logger?.error?.(source, 'Ошибка завершения редактирования ячейки', {
        message: error?.message || String(error)
      });

      if (typeof tableRuntime.abortEditingAsync === 'function') {
        try {
          const cancelled = await tableRuntime.abortEditingAsync();
          return cancelled ? TABLE_EDIT_FINALIZE_RESULT.CANCELLED : TABLE_EDIT_FINALIZE_RESULT.FAILED;
        } catch (abortError) {
          logger?.error?.(source, 'Ошибка отмены редактирования ячейки после неудачного commit', {
            message: abortError?.message || String(abortError)
          });
        }
      }

      return TABLE_EDIT_FINALIZE_RESULT.FAILED;
    }
  }

  return TABLE_EDIT_FINALIZE_RESULT.FAILED;
}


==================================================
FILE: renderer/modules/metagen/tables/finalizeEditingOnContextLeave.js
==================================================

import { METAGEN_CONFIG } from '../metagenConfig.js';
import {
  finalizeActiveTableEditing,
  TABLE_EDIT_FINALIZE_RESULT
} from './finalizeActiveTableEditing.js';

export const TABLE_CONTEXT_FINALIZE_FLOW = {
  CONTINUED: 'continued',
  BLOCKED: 'blocked'
};

function pickOutcome(results) {
  if (results.includes(TABLE_EDIT_FINALIZE_RESULT.FAILED)) {
    return TABLE_EDIT_FINALIZE_RESULT.FAILED;
  }

  if (results.includes(TABLE_EDIT_FINALIZE_RESULT.COMMITTED)) {
    return TABLE_EDIT_FINALIZE_RESULT.COMMITTED;
  }

  if (results.includes(TABLE_EDIT_FINALIZE_RESULT.CANCELLED)) {
    return TABLE_EDIT_FINALIZE_RESULT.CANCELLED;
  }

  return TABLE_EDIT_FINALIZE_RESULT.NO_OP;
}

export async function finalizeEditingOnContextLeave({
  tables = [],
  logger,
  source,
  reason = METAGEN_CONFIG.tableRuntime.transitionReasons.contextLeave,
  blockOnFailure = true
}) {
  if (!Array.isArray(tables) || tables.length === 0) {
    return {
      flow: TABLE_CONTEXT_FINALIZE_FLOW.CONTINUED,
      outcome: TABLE_EDIT_FINALIZE_RESULT.NO_OP,
      reason
    };
  }

  const results = await Promise.all(
    tables.map(({ tableRuntime, contextId }) => finalizeActiveTableEditing({
      tableRuntime,
      logger,
      source: contextId ? `${source}.${contextId}` : source
    }))
  );

  const outcome = pickOutcome(results);

  if (outcome === TABLE_EDIT_FINALIZE_RESULT.FAILED) {
    logger?.error?.(source, 'Не удалось завершить редактирование при потере контекста', {
      reason,
      results
    });

    return {
      flow: blockOnFailure ? TABLE_CONTEXT_FINALIZE_FLOW.BLOCKED : TABLE_CONTEXT_FINALIZE_FLOW.CONTINUED,
      outcome,
      reason
    };
  }

  return {
    flow: TABLE_CONTEXT_FINALIZE_FLOW.CONTINUED,
    outcome,
    reason
  };
}


==================================================
FILE: renderer/modules/metagen/tables/metaGenParamsTableAutoStyle.js
==================================================

import {
  AUTO_STYLE_LOGICAL_EXPANSION_KIND,
  interpretMutatingCommandRefreshDescriptor,
  isMutatingCommand,
  RECOMPUTE_MODE
} from './metaGenParamsTableAutoStyleInterpretation.js';

function normalizeCellValue(cellValue) {
  if (cellValue == null) {
    return '';
  }

  if (typeof cellValue === 'object') {
    if ('v' in cellValue) {
      return normalizeCellValue(cellValue.v);
    }

    return '';
  }

  return String(cellValue).trim();
}

function isRowEmpty(rowValues) {
  return rowValues.every((cellValue) => normalizeCellValue(cellValue) === '');
}

function canAccessCell(sheet, rowIndex, columnIndex) {
  try {
    sheet.getRange(rowIndex, columnIndex, 1, 1);
    return true;
  } catch {
    return false;
  }
}

function resolveSheetDimensionHint(sheet, methodNames) {
  for (const methodName of methodNames) {
    const method = sheet?.[methodName];

    if (typeof method !== 'function') {
      continue;
    }

    const value = Number(method.call(sheet));
    if (Number.isFinite(value) && value > 0) {
      return Math.floor(value);
    }
  }

  return null;
}

function resolveActualRowCount(sheet, currentHint) {
  const directRowCount = resolveSheetDimensionHint(sheet, ['getRowCount', 'getMaxRows', 'getSheetRowCount']);
  if (directRowCount != null) {
    return directRowCount;
  }

  let count = Math.max(1, currentHint);

  while (count > 1 && !canAccessCell(sheet, count - 1, 0)) {
    count -= 1;
  }

  while (canAccessCell(sheet, count, 0)) {
    count += 1;
  }

  return count;
}

function resolveActualColumnCount(sheet, currentHint) {
  const directColumnCount = resolveSheetDimensionHint(sheet, ['getColumnCount', 'getMaxColumns', 'getSheetColumnCount']);
  if (directColumnCount != null) {
    return directColumnCount;
  }

  let count = Math.max(1, currentHint);

  while (count > 1 && !canAccessCell(sheet, 0, count - 1)) {
    count -= 1;
  }

  while (canAccessCell(sheet, 0, count)) {
    count += 1;
  }

  return count;
}

function getRowValues(sheet, rowIndex, actualColumnCount) {
  const safeColumnCount = Math.max(1, actualColumnCount);
  const range = sheet.getRange(rowIndex, 0, 1, safeColumnCount);
  const values = range.getValues();

  if (!Array.isArray(values) || !Array.isArray(values[0])) {
    return new Array(safeColumnCount).fill('');
  }

  return values[0];
}

function findLastNonEmptyRowIndex(sheet, actualRowCount, actualColumnCount) {
  for (let rowIndex = actualRowCount - 1; rowIndex >= 0; rowIndex -= 1) {
    const rowValues = getRowValues(sheet, rowIndex, actualColumnCount);
    if (!isRowEmpty(rowValues)) {
      return rowIndex;
    }
  }

  return -1;
}

function resolveLastRelevantRecomputeRow({
  sheet,
  actualRowCount,
  actualColumnCount,
  minRowIndex
}) {
  const maxRowIndex = Math.max(0, actualRowCount - 1);
  const normalizedMinRowIndex = Number.isInteger(minRowIndex) ? minRowIndex : 0;
  const safeMinRowIndex = Math.max(0, Math.min(normalizedMinRowIndex, maxRowIndex));
  const lastNonEmptyRowIndex = findLastNonEmptyRowIndex(sheet, actualRowCount, actualColumnCount);

  if (lastNonEmptyRowIndex < 0) {
    return safeMinRowIndex;
  }

  return Math.max(safeMinRowIndex, lastNonEmptyRowIndex);
}

function applyRowStyle(univerAPI, sheet, rowIndex, actualColumnCount, rowStyle, borderConfig) {
  if (!canAccessCell(sheet, rowIndex, 0)) {
    return false;
  }

  const rowRange = sheet.getRange(rowIndex, 0, 1, Math.max(1, actualColumnCount));

  rowRange
    .setBackgroundColor(rowStyle.backgroundColor)
    .setFontWeight(rowStyle.fontWeight)
    .setHorizontalAlignment(rowStyle.horizontalAlignment)
    .setVerticalAlignment(rowStyle.verticalAlignment)
    .setBorder(
      univerAPI.Enum.BorderType[borderConfig.type],
      univerAPI.Enum.BorderStyleTypes[borderConfig.style],
      borderConfig.color
    );

  return true;
}

function createDebouncedExecutor(delayMs, callback) {
  let timeoutId = null;

  return {
    schedule() {
      if (timeoutId != null) {
        clearTimeout(timeoutId);
      }

      timeoutId = setTimeout(() => {
        timeoutId = null;
        callback();
      }, delayMs);
    },

    dispose() {
      if (timeoutId != null) {
        clearTimeout(timeoutId);
        timeoutId = null;
      }
    },

    cancel() {
      if (timeoutId != null) {
        clearTimeout(timeoutId);
        timeoutId = null;
      }
    }
  };
}

function mergeBounds(currentBounds, nextBounds) {
  if (!currentBounds) {
    return { ...nextBounds };
  }

  return {
    startRow: Math.min(currentBounds.startRow, nextBounds.startRow),
    endRow: Math.max(currentBounds.endRow, nextBounds.endRow)
  };
}

function mergeRecomputeMode(currentMode, nextMode) {
const priority = {
    [RECOMPUTE_MODE.LOGICAL_BLOCK]: 0,
    [RECOMPUTE_MODE.FROM_ROW_TO_END]: 1,
    [RECOMPUTE_MODE.FULL]: 2
  };

  return priority[nextMode] > priority[currentMode] ? nextMode : currentMode;
}

function getFullRefreshBounds(actualRowCount) {
  return {
    startRow: 0,
    endRow: Math.max(0, actualRowCount - 1)
  };
}

function clampBounds(bounds, actualRowCount) {
  const maxRowIndex = Math.max(0, actualRowCount - 1);
  const startRow = Math.max(0, Math.min(bounds.startRow, maxRowIndex));
  let endRow = Math.max(0, Math.min(bounds.endRow, maxRowIndex));

  if (endRow < startRow) {
    endRow = startRow;
  }

  return { startRow, endRow };
}

function expandBoundsToLogicalBlock(sheet, bounds, actualRowCount, actualColumnCount) {
  let { startRow, endRow } = clampBounds(bounds, actualRowCount);

  while (startRow > 0) {
    const previousRowValues = getRowValues(sheet, startRow - 1, actualColumnCount);

    if (isRowEmpty(previousRowValues)) {
      break;
    }

    startRow -= 1;
  }

  while (endRow + 1 < actualRowCount) {
    const nextRowValues = getRowValues(sheet, endRow + 1, actualColumnCount);
    if (isRowEmpty(nextRowValues)) {
      break;
    }

    endRow += 1;
  }

  return { startRow, endRow };
}

function findLogicalBlockStart(sheet, rowIndex, actualColumnCount) {
  let startRow = rowIndex;

  while (startRow > 0) {
    const previousRowValues = getRowValues(sheet, startRow - 1, actualColumnCount);

    if (isRowEmpty(previousRowValues)) {
      break;
    }

    startRow -= 1;
  }

  return startRow;
}

function findLogicalBlockEnd(sheet, rowIndex, actualRowCount, actualColumnCount) {
  let endRow = rowIndex;

  while (endRow + 1 < actualRowCount) {
    const nextRowValues = getRowValues(sheet, endRow + 1, actualColumnCount);
    if (isRowEmpty(nextRowValues)) {
      break;
    }

    endRow += 1;
  }

  return endRow;
}

function expandRangeBoundsAcrossLogicalBlocks(sheet, bounds, actualRowCount, actualColumnCount) {
  // Preserve explicit affected span as immutable core; only expand outward.
  let { startRow, endRow } = clampBounds(bounds, actualRowCount);

  while (startRow > 0) {
    const previousRowValues = getRowValues(sheet, startRow - 1, actualColumnCount);
    if (isRowEmpty(previousRowValues)) {
      break;
    }
    startRow -= 1;
  }

  while (endRow + 1 < actualRowCount) {
    const nextRowValues = getRowValues(sheet, endRow + 1, actualColumnCount);
    if (isRowEmpty(nextRowValues)) {
      break;
    }
    endRow += 1;
  }

  return { startRow, endRow };
}

function buildRowCategorySnapshot({
  sheet,
  startRow,
  endRow,
  actualColumnCount,
  rowCategoryConfig
}) {
  const snapshot = new Map();
  let previousRowIsNonEmpty = false;

  if (startRow > 0) {
    const previousRowValues = getRowValues(sheet, startRow - 1, actualColumnCount);
    previousRowIsNonEmpty = !isRowEmpty(previousRowValues);
  }

  for (let rowIndex = startRow; rowIndex <= endRow; rowIndex += 1) {
    const rowValues = getRowValues(sheet, rowIndex, actualColumnCount);
    const rowIsEmpty = isRowEmpty(rowValues);

    if (rowIsEmpty) {
      snapshot.set(rowIndex, rowCategoryConfig.empty);
      previousRowIsNonEmpty = false;
      continue;
    }

    snapshot.set(rowIndex, previousRowIsNonEmpty ? rowCategoryConfig.value : rowCategoryConfig.key);
    previousRowIsNonEmpty = true;
  }

  return snapshot;
}

function ensureRowStatesLength(rowStates, targetLength, emptyCategory) {
  while (rowStates.length < targetLength) {
    rowStates.push(emptyCategory);
  }

  if (rowStates.length > targetLength) {
    rowStates.length = targetLength;
  }
}

function trimTrailingEmptyCells(rowValues) {
  const normalized = rowValues.map((value) => normalizeCellValue(value));

  while (normalized.length > 0 && normalized[normalized.length - 1] === '') {
    normalized.pop();
  }

  return normalized;
}

function buildStructuredBlocks(sheet, actualRowCount, actualColumnCount, rowCategoryConfig, rowStates) {
  const blocks = [];
  let currentBlock = null;

  for (let rowIndex = 0; rowIndex < actualRowCount; rowIndex += 1) {
    const category = rowStates[rowIndex] || rowCategoryConfig.empty;
    const rowValues = trimTrailingEmptyCells(getRowValues(sheet, rowIndex, actualColumnCount));

    if (category === rowCategoryConfig.empty) {
      currentBlock = null;
      continue;
    }

    if (category === rowCategoryConfig.key) {
      currentBlock = {
        keyRowIndex: rowIndex,
        valueRowIndexes: [],
        keyValues: rowValues,
        valueRows: []
      };
      blocks.push(currentBlock);
      continue;
    }

    if (currentBlock) {
      currentBlock.valueRowIndexes.push(rowIndex);
      currentBlock.valueRows.push(rowValues);
    }
  }

  return blocks;
}

const AUTO_STYLE_REFRESH_REASON = {
  UNKNOWN: 'unknown',
  INIT: 'init',
  MANUAL_REFRESH: 'manual-refresh',
  REPLAY_REFRESH: 'replay-refresh',
  COMMAND_PARTS_SEPARATOR: ':'
};

function getCommandRefreshReason(commandId, operationKind) {
  return `${commandId}${AUTO_STYLE_REFRESH_REASON.COMMAND_PARTS_SEPARATOR}${operationKind}`;
}

function createAutoStyleRefreshRuntime({
  univerAPI,
  sheet,
  logger,
  source,
  logMessages,
  autoStyleConfig,
  rowCategoryConfig,
  rowCount,
  columnCount
}) {
  let actualRowCount = Math.max(1, rowCount);
  let actualColumnCount = Math.max(1, columnCount);
  let rowStates = Array.from({ length: actualRowCount }, () => rowCategoryConfig.empty);
  let disposed = false;
  let isApplyingAutoStyle = false;

  function syncActualDimensions() {
    actualRowCount = resolveActualRowCount(sheet, actualRowCount);
    actualColumnCount = resolveActualColumnCount(sheet, actualColumnCount);
    ensureRowStatesLength(rowStates, actualRowCount, rowCategoryConfig.empty);
  }

  function applyRowCategoryStyle(rowIndex, rowCategory) {
    const nextStyle = rowCategory === rowCategoryConfig.key
      ? autoStyleConfig.rowStyles.key
      : autoStyleConfig.rowStyles.normal;

    return applyRowStyle(univerAPI, sheet, rowIndex, actualColumnCount, nextStyle, autoStyleConfig.border);
  }

  function refreshBounds(
    bounds,
    mode = RECOMPUTE_MODE.LOGICAL_BLOCK,
    logicalExpansionKind = AUTO_STYLE_LOGICAL_EXPANSION_KIND.ORDINARY,
    options = {}
  ) {
    if (disposed || !bounds) {
      return;
    }

    try {
      isApplyingAutoStyle = true;
      syncActualDimensions();
      let logicalBounds;
      if (mode === RECOMPUTE_MODE.FULL) {
        logicalBounds = {
          startRow: 0,
          endRow: resolveLastRelevantRecomputeRow({
            sheet,
            actualRowCount,
            actualColumnCount,
            minRowIndex: 0
          })
        };
      } else if (mode === RECOMPUTE_MODE.FROM_ROW_TO_END) {
        const clamped = clampBounds(bounds, actualRowCount);
        logicalBounds = {
          startRow: clamped.startRow,
          endRow: resolveLastRelevantRecomputeRow({
            sheet,
            actualRowCount,
            actualColumnCount,
            minRowIndex: Math.max(clamped.startRow, clamped.endRow)
          })
        };
      } else {
        const clampedBounds = clampBounds(bounds, actualRowCount);
        logicalBounds = logicalExpansionKind === AUTO_STYLE_LOGICAL_EXPANSION_KIND.RANGE
          ? expandRangeBoundsAcrossLogicalBlocks(sheet, clampedBounds, actualRowCount, actualColumnCount)
          : expandBoundsToLogicalBlock(sheet, clampedBounds, actualRowCount, actualColumnCount);
      }

      const snapshot = buildRowCategorySnapshot({
        sheet,
        startRow: logicalBounds.startRow,
        endRow: logicalBounds.endRow,
        actualColumnCount,
        rowCategoryConfig
      });

      let changedRowsCount = 0;
      let styledRowsCount = 0;
      let skippedRowsCount = 0;
      const restyleUnchangedRows = options.restyleUnchangedRows !== false;

      if (mode === RECOMPUTE_MODE.FULL) {
        for (let rowIndex = 0; rowIndex < actualRowCount; rowIndex += 1) {
          rowStates[rowIndex] = rowCategoryConfig.empty;
        }
      }

      for (const [rowIndex, nextCategory] of snapshot.entries()) {
        const hasCategoryChanged = rowStates[rowIndex] !== nextCategory;
        if (hasCategoryChanged) {
          changedRowsCount += 1;
          rowStates[rowIndex] = nextCategory;
        }

        if (!hasCategoryChanged && !restyleUnchangedRows) {
          continue;
        }

        if (applyRowCategoryStyle(rowIndex, nextCategory)) {
          styledRowsCount += 1;
        } else {
          skippedRowsCount += 1;
        }
      }

      logger.info(source, logMessages.paramsAutoStyleApplied, {
        mode,
        logicalExpansionKind,
        restyleUnchangedRows,
        bounds: logicalBounds,
        changedRowsCount,
        styledRowsCount,
        skippedRowsCount,
        actualRowCount,
        actualColumnCount
      });
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error(source, logMessages.paramsAutoStyleFailed, error);
    } finally {
      isApplyingAutoStyle = false;
    }
  }

  function getRowCategory(rowIndex) {
    return rowStates[rowIndex] || rowCategoryConfig.empty;
  }

  function getStructuredBlocks() {
    syncActualDimensions();
    return buildStructuredBlocks(sheet, actualRowCount, actualColumnCount, rowCategoryConfig, rowStates);
  }

  return {
    refreshBounds,
    getRowCategory,
    getStructuredBlocks,
    getActualRowCount: () => actualRowCount,
    isApplyingAutoStyle: () => isApplyingAutoStyle,
    dispose() {
      disposed = true;
    }
  };
}

export function createMetaGenParamsTableAutoStyle({
  univerAPI,
  workbook,
  sheet,
  logger,
  source,
  logMessages,
  rowCount,
  columnCount,
  autoStyleConfig
}) {
  const rowCategoryConfig = autoStyleConfig.rowCategory;
  const refreshRuntime = createAutoStyleRefreshRuntime({
    univerAPI,
    sheet,
    logger,
    source,
    logMessages,
    autoStyleConfig,
    rowCategoryConfig,
    rowCount,
    columnCount
  });

  let pendingBounds = null;
  let pendingRecomputeMode = RECOMPUTE_MODE.LOGICAL_BLOCK;
  let pendingLogicalExpansionKind = AUTO_STYLE_LOGICAL_EXPANSION_KIND.ORDINARY;
  let pendingRestyleUnchangedRows = true;
  let replaySuppressionDepth = 0;

  function resetPendingRefreshState() {
    pendingBounds = null;
    pendingRecomputeMode = RECOMPUTE_MODE.LOGICAL_BLOCK;
    pendingLogicalExpansionKind = AUTO_STYLE_LOGICAL_EXPANSION_KIND.ORDINARY;
    pendingRestyleUnchangedRows = true;
  }

  const debouncedRefresh = createDebouncedExecutor(autoStyleConfig.debounceDelayMs, () => {
    const mode = pendingRecomputeMode;
    const logicalExpansionKind = pendingLogicalExpansionKind;
    const boundsToRefresh = pendingBounds || {
      startRow: 0,
      endRow: Math.max(0, refreshRuntime.getActualRowCount() - 1)
    };
    const restyleUnchangedRows = pendingRestyleUnchangedRows;

    resetPendingRefreshState();
    refreshRuntime.refreshBounds(boundsToRefresh, mode, logicalExpansionKind, { restyleUnchangedRows });
  });

  function scheduleRefresh(bounds, reason = AUTO_STYLE_REFRESH_REASON.UNKNOWN, options = {}) {
    const mode = options.mode || RECOMPUTE_MODE.LOGICAL_BLOCK;
    const logicalExpansionKind = options.logicalExpansionKind || AUTO_STYLE_LOGICAL_EXPANSION_KIND.ORDINARY;
    const restyleUnchangedRows = options.restyleUnchangedRows !== false;
    pendingRecomputeMode = mergeRecomputeMode(pendingRecomputeMode, mode);
    if (logicalExpansionKind === AUTO_STYLE_LOGICAL_EXPANSION_KIND.RANGE) {
      pendingLogicalExpansionKind = AUTO_STYLE_LOGICAL_EXPANSION_KIND.RANGE;
    }
    pendingRestyleUnchangedRows = pendingBounds == null
      ? restyleUnchangedRows
      : (pendingRestyleUnchangedRows || restyleUnchangedRows);

    if (pendingRecomputeMode === RECOMPUTE_MODE.FULL) {
      pendingBounds = getFullRefreshBounds(refreshRuntime.getActualRowCount());
    } else {
      pendingBounds = mergeBounds(pendingBounds, {
        startRow: Math.max(0, bounds.startRow),
        endRow: Math.max(0, bounds.endRow)
      });
    }

    logger.info(source, logMessages.paramsAutoStyleRefreshScheduled, {
      reason,
      mode: pendingRecomputeMode,
      logicalExpansionKind: pendingLogicalExpansionKind,
      restyleUnchangedRows: pendingRestyleUnchangedRows,
      bounds: pendingBounds
    });
    debouncedRefresh.schedule();
  }

  const commandDisposable = workbook.onCommandExecuted((command) => {
    if (refreshRuntime.isApplyingAutoStyle() || replaySuppressionDepth > 0) {
      return;
    }

    const commandId = String(command?.id || 'unknown');
    if (!isMutatingCommand(commandId, autoStyleConfig)) {
      return;
    }

    const refreshDescriptor = interpretMutatingCommandRefreshDescriptor(
      command,
      workbook,
      refreshRuntime.getActualRowCount(),
      autoStyleConfig
    );
    scheduleRefresh(
      refreshDescriptor.bounds,
      getCommandRefreshReason(commandId, refreshDescriptor.operationKind),
      { mode: refreshDescriptor.mode, logicalExpansionKind: refreshDescriptor.logicalExpansionKind }
    );
  });

  scheduleRefresh(
    { startRow: 0, endRow: Math.max(0, refreshRuntime.getActualRowCount() - 1) },
    AUTO_STYLE_REFRESH_REASON.INIT,
    { mode: RECOMPUTE_MODE.FULL, restyleUnchangedRows: false }
  );
  logger.info(source, logMessages.paramsAutoStyleInit);

  function refreshAll() {
    scheduleRefresh(
      { startRow: 0, endRow: Math.max(0, refreshRuntime.getActualRowCount() - 1) },
      AUTO_STYLE_REFRESH_REASON.MANUAL_REFRESH
    );
  }

  function beginReplaySuppression() {
    replaySuppressionDepth += 1;
  }

  function endReplaySuppression() {
    replaySuppressionDepth = Math.max(0, replaySuppressionDepth - 1);
  }

  function refreshReplayBounds(bounds, options = {}) {
    if (!bounds) {
      return;
    }

    debouncedRefresh.cancel();
    resetPendingRefreshState();
    refreshRuntime.refreshBounds(
      bounds,
      options.mode || RECOMPUTE_MODE.LOGICAL_BLOCK,
      options.logicalExpansionKind || AUTO_STYLE_LOGICAL_EXPANSION_KIND.RANGE,
      { restyleUnchangedRows: options.restyleUnchangedRows !== false }
    );

    logger.info(source, logMessages.paramsAutoStyleRefreshScheduled, {
      reason: AUTO_STYLE_REFRESH_REASON.REPLAY_REFRESH,
      mode: options.mode || RECOMPUTE_MODE.LOGICAL_BLOCK,
      logicalExpansionKind: options.logicalExpansionKind || AUTO_STYLE_LOGICAL_EXPANSION_KIND.RANGE,
      restyleUnchangedRows: options.restyleUnchangedRows !== false,
      bounds
    });
  }

  function dispose() {
    refreshRuntime.dispose();
    commandDisposable?.dispose?.();
    debouncedRefresh.dispose();
  }

  return {
    getRowCategory: refreshRuntime.getRowCategory,
    getStructuredBlocks: refreshRuntime.getStructuredBlocks,
    refreshAll,
    beginReplaySuppression,
    endReplaySuppression,
    refreshReplayBounds,
    dispose
  };
}


==================================================
FILE: renderer/modules/metagen/tables/metaGenParamsTableAutoStyleInterpretation.js
==================================================

export const RECOMPUTE_MODE = {
  LOGICAL_BLOCK: 'logical-block',
  FROM_ROW_TO_END: 'from-row-to-end',
  FULL: 'full'
};

export const AUTO_STYLE_OPERATION_KIND = {
  STRUCTURAL: 'structural',
  ORDINARY: 'ordinary',
  RANGE: 'range'
};

export const AUTO_STYLE_LOGICAL_EXPANSION_KIND = {
  ORDINARY: 'ordinary',
  RANGE: 'range'
};

const AMBIGUOUS_CUT_MOVE_COMMAND_ID_FRAGMENTS = [
  'cut',
  'move-row',
  'move-rows',
  'move-range',
  'delete-range-move-up',
  'insert-range-move-down'
];

const EXPLICIT_STRUCTURAL_MOVE_COMMAND_ID_FRAGMENTS = [
  'move-row',
  'move-rows',
  'move-range',
  'delete-range-move-up',
  'insert-range-move-down'
];

const ROW_INDEXED_CONTAINER_KEY_FRAGMENTS = [
  'cellvalue',
  'cellvalues',
  'cellvaluemap',
  'valuemap',
  'rangemap',
  'rangecell',
  'rangevalue'
];

function collectRowBoundsFromUnknownShape(value, depthLeft, rowBoundsList, keyPath = []) {
  if (depthLeft < 0 || value == null) {
    return;
  }

  if (Array.isArray(value)) {
    value.forEach((item) => collectRowBoundsFromUnknownShape(item, depthLeft - 1, rowBoundsList, keyPath));
    return;
  }

  if (typeof value !== 'object') {
    return;
  }

  const toInteger = (candidate) => {
    if (candidate == null) {
      return null;
    }

    if (typeof candidate === 'string') {
      const trimmed = candidate.trim();

      if (trimmed === '') {
        return null;
      }

      const parsed = Number(trimmed);
      return Number.isInteger(parsed) ? parsed : null;
    }

    return Number.isInteger(candidate) ? candidate : null;
  };
  const firstInteger = (objectValue, keys) => {
    for (const key of keys) {
      const parsed = toInteger(objectValue[key]);

      if (parsed != null) {
        return parsed;
      }
    }

    return null;
  };

  const startRow = firstInteger(value, ['startRow', 'startRowIndex', 'rowStart', 'fromRow']);
  const endRow = firstInteger(value, ['endRow', 'endRowIndex', 'rowEnd', 'toRow']);
  const row = firstInteger(value, ['row', 'rowIndex']);
  const rowCount = firstInteger(value, ['rowCount', 'rows', 'numRows', 'rowSpan', 'rowSize', 'height']);
  const parentKey = String(keyPath[keyPath.length - 1] || '').toLowerCase();
  const inRowIndexedContainer = ROW_INDEXED_CONTAINER_KEY_FRAGMENTS.some((fragment) =>
    parentKey.includes(fragment)
  );
  const hasRange = startRow != null && endRow != null;
  const hasStartAndCount = startRow != null && rowCount != null && rowCount > 0;
  const hasRowAndCount = row != null && rowCount != null && rowCount > 0;

  if (hasRange) {
    rowBoundsList.push({
      startRow: Math.min(startRow, endRow),
      endRow: Math.max(startRow, endRow)
    });
  } else if (hasStartAndCount) {
    rowBoundsList.push({
      startRow,
      endRow: startRow + rowCount - 1
    });
  } else if (hasRowAndCount) {
    rowBoundsList.push({
      startRow: row,
      endRow: row + rowCount - 1
    });
  } else if (row != null) {
    rowBoundsList.push({ startRow: row, endRow: row });
  }

  if (inRowIndexedContainer) {
    const numericRowKeys = Object.keys(value)
      .map((key) => {
        if (!/^-?\d+$/.test(key)) {
          return null;
        }

        const parsed = Number(key);
        return Number.isInteger(parsed) ? parsed : null;
      })
      .filter((key) => key != null);

    if (numericRowKeys.length > 0) {
      rowBoundsList.push({
        startRow: Math.min(...numericRowKeys),
        endRow: Math.max(...numericRowKeys)
      });
    }
  }

  Object.entries(value).forEach(([nestedKey, nestedValue]) => {
    collectRowBoundsFromUnknownShape(nestedValue, depthLeft - 1, rowBoundsList, [...keyPath, nestedKey]);
  });
}

function getFallbackBoundsFromActiveSelection(workbook) {
  try {
    const activeSheet = workbook.getActiveSheet();
    const activeRange = activeSheet.getActiveRange();

    if (!activeRange) {
      return null;
    }

    const rangeInfo = activeRange.getRange();

    if (rangeInfo && Number.isInteger(rangeInfo.startRow) && Number.isInteger(rangeInfo.endRow)) {
      return {
        startRow: rangeInfo.startRow,
        endRow: rangeInfo.endRow
      };
    }
  } catch {
    return null;
  }

  return null;
}

function collectCommandRowBounds(command, config) {
  const rowBoundsList = [];
  collectRowBoundsFromUnknownShape(command?.params, config.maxRecursiveRangeDepth, rowBoundsList);
  return rowBoundsList;
}

function commandIdHasAnyFragment(commandId, fragments) {
  const normalizedCommandId = String(commandId || '').toLowerCase();

  if (normalizedCommandId === '') {
    return false;
  }

  return fragments.some((fragment) => normalizedCommandId.includes(fragment));
}

function isAmbiguousCutMoveCommand(commandId) {
  return commandIdHasAnyFragment(commandId, AMBIGUOUS_CUT_MOVE_COMMAND_ID_FRAGMENTS);
}

function isExplicitStructuralMoveCommand(commandId) {
  return commandIdHasAnyFragment(commandId, EXPLICIT_STRUCTURAL_MOVE_COMMAND_ID_FRAGMENTS);
}

function hasCutMoveIntentFromParams(value, depthLeft) {
  if (depthLeft < 0 || value == null) {
    return false;
  }

  if (Array.isArray(value)) {
    return value.some((item) => hasCutMoveIntentFromParams(item, depthLeft - 1));
  }

  if (typeof value === 'string') {
    return false;
  }

  if (typeof value !== 'object') {
    return false;
  }

  if (value.isCut === true || value.isMove === true) {
    return true;
  }

  const semanticKeys = ['type', 'operation', 'action', 'pasteType', 'copyType', 'mode', 'kind'];
  for (const key of semanticKeys) {
    if (typeof value[key] === 'string') {
      const normalized = value[key].toLowerCase();
      if (normalized.includes('cut') || normalized.includes('move')) {
        return true;
      }
    }
  }

  return Object.values(value).some((nestedValue) =>
    hasCutMoveIntentFromParams(nestedValue, depthLeft - 1)
  );
}

function mergeRowBoundsList(rowBoundsList) {
  if (rowBoundsList.length === 0) {
    return null;
  }

  return rowBoundsList.reduce((accumulator, currentBounds) => ({
    startRow: Math.min(accumulator.startRow, currentBounds.startRow),
    endRow: Math.max(accumulator.endRow, currentBounds.endRow)
  }));
}

function isRangeBounds(rowBoundsList) {
  if (rowBoundsList.length > 1) {
    return true;
  }

  return rowBoundsList.some((bounds) => bounds.endRow > bounds.startRow);
}

function resolveEarliestKnownStartRow(mergedRowBounds, fallbackBounds) {
  if (mergedRowBounds && fallbackBounds) {
    return Math.min(mergedRowBounds.startRow, fallbackBounds.startRow);
  }

  if (mergedRowBounds) {
    return mergedRowBounds.startRow;
  }

  if (fallbackBounds) {
    return fallbackBounds.startRow;
  }

  return null;
}

function getBoundsFromRowCountHint(rowCountHint) {
  return {
    startRow: 0,
    endRow: Math.max(0, rowCountHint - 1)
  };
}

function toNonNegativeBounds(bounds) {
  return {
    startRow: Math.max(0, bounds.startRow),
    endRow: Math.max(0, bounds.endRow)
  };
}

function createCommandRefreshInterpretationContext(command, config) {
  const commandId = String(command?.id || '');
  const normalizedCommandId = commandId.toLowerCase();
  const rowBoundsList = collectCommandRowBounds(command, config);
  const mergedRowBounds = mergeRowBoundsList(rowBoundsList);
  const cutMoveLikeCommand = isAmbiguousCutMoveCommand(commandId) ||
    hasCutMoveIntentFromParams(command?.params, config.maxRecursiveRangeDepth);
  const explicitMoveCommand = isExplicitStructuralMoveCommand(commandId);
  const clipboardCutLikeCommand = cutMoveLikeCommand && !explicitMoveCommand;
  const hasReliableSourceAndDestinationBounds = rowBoundsList.length > 1;
  const mergedBoundsAreRange = mergedRowBounds != null && mergedRowBounds.endRow > mergedRowBounds.startRow;
  const shouldTreatCutLikeAsBoundedRange = clipboardCutLikeCommand &&
    (hasReliableSourceAndDestinationBounds || mergedBoundsAreRange);

  return {
    commandId,
    normalizedCommandId,
    rowBoundsList,
    mergedRowBounds,
    cutMoveLikeCommand,
    clipboardCutLikeCommand,
    mergedBoundsAreRange,
    shouldTreatCutLikeAsBoundedRange
  };
}

function resolveLogicalExpansionKind(operationKind, mode) {
  if (mode !== RECOMPUTE_MODE.LOGICAL_BLOCK) {
    return AUTO_STYLE_LOGICAL_EXPANSION_KIND.ORDINARY;
  }

  return operationKind === AUTO_STYLE_OPERATION_KIND.RANGE
    ? AUTO_STYLE_LOGICAL_EXPANSION_KIND.RANGE
    : AUTO_STYLE_LOGICAL_EXPANSION_KIND.ORDINARY;
}

function createRefreshDescriptor(operationKind, mode, bounds) {
  return {
    operationKind,
    mode,
    bounds,
    logicalExpansionKind: resolveLogicalExpansionKind(operationKind, mode)
  };
}

function resolveFullRefreshDescriptor(context, workbook, rowCountHint, config) {
  if (!isFullRefreshCommand(context.commandId, config)) {
    return null;
  }

  if (context.mergedRowBounds) {
    return createRefreshDescriptor(
      AUTO_STYLE_OPERATION_KIND.STRUCTURAL,
      RECOMPUTE_MODE.FROM_ROW_TO_END,
      toNonNegativeBounds(context.mergedRowBounds)
    );
  }

  const fallbackBounds = getFallbackBoundsFromActiveSelection(workbook);
  if (fallbackBounds) {
    return createRefreshDescriptor(
      AUTO_STYLE_OPERATION_KIND.STRUCTURAL,
      RECOMPUTE_MODE.FROM_ROW_TO_END,
      toNonNegativeBounds(fallbackBounds)
    );
  }

  return createRefreshDescriptor(
    AUTO_STYLE_OPERATION_KIND.STRUCTURAL,
    RECOMPUTE_MODE.FULL,
    getBoundsFromRowCountHint(rowCountHint)
  );
}

function resolveDescriptorWithoutMergedBounds(context, workbook, rowCountHint) {
  if (context.mergedRowBounds) {
    return null;
  }

  const fallbackBounds = getFallbackBoundsFromActiveSelection(workbook);
  if (context.cutMoveLikeCommand) {
    if (fallbackBounds) {
      return createRefreshDescriptor(
        AUTO_STYLE_OPERATION_KIND.STRUCTURAL,
        RECOMPUTE_MODE.FROM_ROW_TO_END,
        toNonNegativeBounds(fallbackBounds)
      );
    }

    return createRefreshDescriptor(
      AUTO_STYLE_OPERATION_KIND.STRUCTURAL,
      RECOMPUTE_MODE.FULL,
      getBoundsFromRowCountHint(rowCountHint)
    );
  }

  if (fallbackBounds) {
    return createRefreshDescriptor(
      AUTO_STYLE_OPERATION_KIND.ORDINARY,
      RECOMPUTE_MODE.LOGICAL_BLOCK,
      toNonNegativeBounds(fallbackBounds)
    );
  }

  return createRefreshDescriptor(
    AUTO_STYLE_OPERATION_KIND.ORDINARY,
    RECOMPUTE_MODE.FULL,
    getBoundsFromRowCountHint(rowCountHint)
  );
}

function resolveUnboundedCutLikeDescriptor(context, workbook, rowCountHint) {
  if (!context.mergedRowBounds || !context.cutMoveLikeCommand || context.shouldTreatCutLikeAsBoundedRange) {
    return null;
  }

  const fallbackBounds = context.clipboardCutLikeCommand
    ? getFallbackBoundsFromActiveSelection(workbook)
    : null;
  const earliestKnownStartRow = resolveEarliestKnownStartRow(context.mergedRowBounds, fallbackBounds);
  const knownEndRow = fallbackBounds
    ? Math.max(context.mergedRowBounds.endRow, fallbackBounds.endRow)
    : context.mergedRowBounds.endRow;

  const mode = earliestKnownStartRow == null ? RECOMPUTE_MODE.FULL : RECOMPUTE_MODE.FROM_ROW_TO_END;
  const bounds = earliestKnownStartRow == null
    ? getBoundsFromRowCountHint(rowCountHint)
    : {
        startRow: Math.max(0, earliestKnownStartRow),
        endRow: Math.max(0, knownEndRow)
      };

  return createRefreshDescriptor(AUTO_STYLE_OPERATION_KIND.STRUCTURAL, mode, bounds);
}

function resolveLogicalBoundsDescriptor(context) {
  const hasMultiRowOrMultiFragmentBounds = context.rowBoundsList.length > 1 || context.mergedBoundsAreRange;
  const isSetRangeValuesCommand = context.normalizedCommandId.includes('set-range-values');
  const operationKind = (isSetRangeValuesCommand && hasMultiRowOrMultiFragmentBounds) ||
    isRangeBounds(context.rowBoundsList)
    ? AUTO_STYLE_OPERATION_KIND.RANGE
    : AUTO_STYLE_OPERATION_KIND.ORDINARY;

  return createRefreshDescriptor(
    operationKind,
    RECOMPUTE_MODE.LOGICAL_BLOCK,
    toNonNegativeBounds(context.mergedRowBounds)
  );
}

function createRefreshDescriptorFromContext(context, workbook, rowCountHint, config) {
  return resolveFullRefreshDescriptor(context, workbook, rowCountHint, config) ||
    resolveDescriptorWithoutMergedBounds(context, workbook, rowCountHint) ||
    resolveUnboundedCutLikeDescriptor(context, workbook, rowCountHint) ||
    resolveLogicalBoundsDescriptor(context);
}

export function isFullRefreshCommand(commandId, config) {
  const normalizedCommandId = String(commandId || '').toLowerCase();

  return config.fullRefreshCommandIdIncludes.some((fragment) =>
    normalizedCommandId.includes(fragment)
  );
}

export function isMutatingCommand(commandId, config) {
  const normalizedCommandId = String(commandId || '').toLowerCase();

  if (normalizedCommandId === '') {
    return false;
  }

  if (isFullRefreshCommand(normalizedCommandId, config)) {
    return true;
  }

  const mutatingFragments = Array.isArray(config.mutatingCommandIdIncludes)
    ? config.mutatingCommandIdIncludes
    : [];

  return mutatingFragments.some((fragment) =>
    normalizedCommandId.includes(fragment)
  );
}

export function interpretMutatingCommandRefreshDescriptor(command, workbook, rowCountHint, config) {
  const interpretationContext = createCommandRefreshInterpretationContext(command, config);
  return createRefreshDescriptorFromContext(interpretationContext, workbook, rowCountHint, config);
}


==================================================
FILE: renderer/modules/metagen/tables/sheetSnapshot.js
==================================================

import { METAGEN_CONFIG } from '../metagenConfig.js';

export function serializeSheetCellValue(cellValue) {
  if (cellValue == null) {
    return '';
  }

  if (typeof cellValue === 'object' && 'v' in cellValue) {
    return serializeSheetCellValue(cellValue.v);
  }

  if (typeof cellValue === 'object') {
    return '';
  }

  if (typeof cellValue === 'string' || typeof cellValue === 'number' || typeof cellValue === 'boolean') {
    return cellValue;
  }

  return String(cellValue);
}

export function readSheetMatrix(sheet, startRow, rowCount, columnCount) {
  const rows = [];

  for (let rowOffset = 0; rowOffset < rowCount; rowOffset += 1) {
    const rowValues = sheet.getRange(startRow + rowOffset, 0, 1, columnCount).getValues()?.[0] || [];
    const snapshotRow = [];

    for (let columnIndex = 0; columnIndex < columnCount; columnIndex += 1) {
      snapshotRow.push(serializeSheetCellValue(rowValues[columnIndex]));
    }

    rows.push(snapshotRow);
  }

  return rows;
}

function canReadRange(sheet, startRow, startColumn, rowCount, columnCount) {
  if (!sheet || startRow < 0 || startColumn < 0 || rowCount <= 0 || columnCount <= 0) {
    return false;
  }

  try {
    sheet.getRange(startRow, startColumn, rowCount, columnCount);
    return true;
  } catch {
    return false;
  }
}

function resolveSafeColumnCountForRow(sheet, rowIndex, maxColumns) {
  if (maxColumns <= 0 || !canReadRange(sheet, rowIndex, 0, 1, 1)) {
    return 0;
  }

  let low = 1;
  let high = maxColumns;
  let best = 1;

  while (low <= high) {
    const middle = Math.floor((low + high) / 2);

    if (canReadRange(sheet, rowIndex, 0, 1, middle)) {
      best = middle;
      low = middle + 1;
    } else {
      high = middle - 1;
    }
  }

  return best;
}

function readSheetRowSafely(sheet, rowIndex, maxColumns) {
  const safeColumnCount = resolveSafeColumnCountForRow(sheet, rowIndex, maxColumns);

  if (safeColumnCount <= 0) {
    return [];
  }

  const rowValues = sheet.getRange(rowIndex, 0, 1, safeColumnCount).getValues()?.[0] || [];
  const normalizedRow = [];

  for (let columnIndex = 0; columnIndex < safeColumnCount; columnIndex += 1) {
    normalizedRow.push(serializeSheetCellValue(rowValues[columnIndex]));
  }

  return normalizedRow;
}

function isEmptyCellValue(value) {
  return value === '';
}

function isEmptyRow(row = []) {
  return !Array.isArray(row) || row.every((cell) => isEmptyCellValue(cell));
}

export function trimTrailingEmptyCells(row = []) {
  if (!Array.isArray(row) || row.length === 0) {
    return [];
  }

  let endIndex = row.length;

  while (endIndex > 0 && isEmptyCellValue(row[endIndex - 1])) {
    endIndex -= 1;
  }

  return row.slice(0, endIndex);
}

export function trimTrailingEmptyRows(rows = []) {
  if (!Array.isArray(rows) || rows.length === 0) {
    return [];
  }

  let endIndex = rows.length;

  while (endIndex > 0 && isEmptyRow(rows[endIndex - 1])) {
    endIndex -= 1;
  }

  return rows.slice(0, endIndex);
}

export function getSheetActualRowCount(sheet, { maxRows = 0, maxColumns = 0 } = {}) {
  if (!sheet || maxRows <= 0 || maxColumns <= 0) {
    return 0;
  }

  for (let rowIndex = maxRows - 1; rowIndex >= 0; rowIndex -= 1) {
    if (!canReadRange(sheet, rowIndex, 0, 1, 1)) {
      continue;
    }

    const rowValues = readSheetRowSafely(sheet, rowIndex, maxColumns);

    if (!isEmptyRow(rowValues)) {
      return rowIndex + 1;
    }
  }

  return 0;
}

export function getSheetActualColumnCount(sheet, { maxRows = 0, maxColumns = 0 } = {}) {
  if (!sheet || maxRows <= 0 || maxColumns <= 0) {
    return 0;
  }

  for (let columnIndex = maxColumns - 1; columnIndex >= 0; columnIndex -= 1) {
    let hasValue = false;

    for (let rowIndex = 0; rowIndex < maxRows; rowIndex += 1) {
      if (!canReadRange(sheet, rowIndex, 0, 1, 1)) {
        continue;
      }

      const rowValues = readSheetRowSafely(sheet, rowIndex, maxColumns);

      if (!isEmptyCellValue(rowValues[columnIndex] ?? '')) {
        hasValue = true;
        break;
      }
    }

    if (hasValue) {
      return columnIndex + 1;
    }
  }

  return 0;
}

export function readTrimmedSheetMatrix(sheet, { maxRows = 0, maxColumns = 0 } = {}) {
  const actualRowCount = getSheetActualRowCount(sheet, { maxRows, maxColumns });

  if (actualRowCount <= 0) {
    return [];
  }

  const actualColumnCount = getSheetActualColumnCount(sheet, { maxRows: actualRowCount, maxColumns });

  if (actualColumnCount <= 0) {
    return [];
  }

  const matrix = [];

  for (let rowIndex = 0; rowIndex < actualRowCount; rowIndex += 1) {
    if (!canReadRange(sheet, rowIndex, 0, 1, 1)) {
      matrix.push(new Array(actualColumnCount).fill(''));
      continue;
    }

    const rowValues = readSheetRowSafely(sheet, rowIndex, actualColumnCount);
    const paddedRow = [];

    for (let columnIndex = 0; columnIndex < actualColumnCount; columnIndex += 1) {
      paddedRow.push(serializeSheetCellValue(rowValues[columnIndex] ?? ''));
    }

    matrix.push(paddedRow);
  }

  const rowsWithoutTrailingEmptyRows = trimTrailingEmptyRows(matrix);

  return rowsWithoutTrailingEmptyRows.map((row) => trimTrailingEmptyCells(row));
}

export function readHeaderPlusRowsDocument(sheet, { maxRows = 0, maxColumns = 0 } = {}) {
  const matrix = readTrimmedSheetMatrix(sheet, { maxRows, maxColumns });

  if (matrix.length === 0) {
    return {
      format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.headerPlusRows,
      header: [],
      rows: []
    };
  }

  return {
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.headerPlusRows,
    header: trimTrailingEmptyCells(matrix[0] || []),
    rows: trimTrailingEmptyRows((matrix.slice(1) || []).map((row) => trimTrailingEmptyCells(row)))
  };
}

export function readTableDocument(sheet, { maxRows = 0, maxColumns = 0, columns = [] } = {}) {
  const matrix = readTrimmedSheetMatrix(sheet, { maxRows, maxColumns });
  const normalizedColumns = Array.isArray(columns) ? [...columns] : [];

  return {
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.table,
    columns: normalizedColumns,
    rows: trimTrailingEmptyRows(matrix)
  };
}

      throw new Error(`${METALAB_CONFIG.commands.createScenario} будет подключена на следующем шаге`);
    },

    [METALAB_CONFIG.commands.runScenario]: async () => {
      throw new Error(`${METALAB_CONFIG.commands.runScenario} будет подключена на следующем шаге`);
    },

    [METALAB_CONFIG.commands.stopScenario]: async () => {
      throw new Error(`${METALAB_CONFIG.commands.stopScenario} будет подключена на следующем шаге`);
    }
  };
}

==================================================
FILE: renderer/modules/metalab/metalabModule.js
==================================================

import { APP_CONFIG } from '../../../config/app-config.js';
import { METALAB_CONFIG } from './metalabConfig.js';
import { createMetaLabDocument } from './metalabDocumentFactory.js';
import { createMetaLabEditor } from '../../editors/metalab/createMetaLabEditor.js';
import { slugifyDocumentName } from '../../runtime/naming.js';

export function createMetaLabModule() {
  return {
    id: METALAB_CONFIG.moduleId,
    name: METALAB_CONFIG.moduleName,
    documentKinds: [METALAB_CONFIG.documentKind],

    getDefaultName() {
      return METALAB_CONFIG.defaults.newDocumentName;
    },

    createDefaultDocument({ name }) {
      return createMetaLabDocument({ name });
    },

    getFileName(document) {
      return `${slugifyDocumentName(document?.scenario?.name || METALAB_CONFIG.defaults.newDocumentName)}${APP_CONFIG.project.fileExtensions.default}`;
    },

    async openDocument({ documentRecord, mountElement }) {
      return createMetaLabEditor({ documentRecord, mountElement });
    }
  };
}

export function createMetaViewDocument({ name = METAVIEW_CONFIG.defaults.newDocumentName } = {}) {
  const safeName = String(name || METAVIEW_CONFIG.defaults.newDocumentName).trim();

  return {
    kind: METAVIEW_CONFIG.documentKind,
    version: METAVIEW_CONFIG.documentSchemaVersion,
    screen: {

    name: METAVIEW_CONFIG.moduleName,
    documentKinds: [METAVIEW_CONFIG.documentKind],
