﻿from pydantic import ValidationError

from runtime_backend.app.core.constants import COMMANDS, ERROR_CODES
from runtime_backend.app.models.command import CommandRequest, CommandResponse
from runtime_backend.app.services import project_catalog
from runtime_backend.app.services.errors import (
    ProjectCreateIssue,
    ProjectDeleteIssue,
    ProjectExportIssue,
    ProjectNotFoundIssue,
    ProjectOpenIssue,
    ProjectSaveIssue,
    ValidationIssue,
)
from runtime_backend.app.services.project_storage import ProjectStorageService

project_storage_service = ProjectStorageService()


def make_ok_response(request_id: str, result: dict) -> CommandResponse:
    return CommandResponse(requestId=request_id, ok=True, result=result)


def make_error_response(request_id: str, code: str, message: str, details: dict | None = None) -> CommandResponse:
    return CommandResponse(
        requestId=request_id,
        ok=False,
        error={
            'code': code,
            'message': message,
            'details': details,
        },
    )


def dispatch_command(request: CommandRequest) -> CommandResponse:
    try:
        platform_module = COMMANDS['platform']['module']
        if request.module != platform_module:
            raise ValidationIssue('Unsupported module', {'module': request.module})

        if request.command == COMMANDS['platform']['list_projects']:
            return make_ok_response(request.request_id, project_catalog.list_projects())

        if request.command == COMMANDS['platform']['create_project']:
            return make_ok_response(request.request_id, project_catalog.create_project(request.payload))

        if request.command == COMMANDS['platform']['open_project']:
            return make_ok_response(request.request_id, project_storage_service.open_project_snapshot(request.payload))

        if request.command == COMMANDS['platform']['delete_project']:
            return make_ok_response(request.request_id, project_catalog.delete_project(request.payload))

        if request.command == COMMANDS['platform']['save_all']:
            return make_ok_response(request.request_id, project_storage_service.save_project_snapshot(request.payload))

        if request.command == COMMANDS['platform']['save_project_as']:
            return make_ok_response(request.request_id, project_storage_service.save_project_snapshot_as(request.payload))

        if request.command == COMMANDS['platform']['export_project']:
            return make_ok_response(request.request_id, project_storage_service.export_project_archive(request.payload))

        raise ValidationIssue(
            'Unsupported command',
            {'module': request.module, 'command': request.command},
        )
    except ValidationIssue as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request.request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['validation'],
            str(error),
            error.details,
        )
    except ProjectCreateIssue as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request.request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['project_create_failed'],
            str(error),
            error.details,
        )
    except ProjectNotFoundIssue as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request.request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['project_not_found'],
            str(error),
            error.details,
        )
    except ProjectOpenIssue as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request.request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['project_open_failed'],
            str(error),
            error.details,
        )
    except ProjectSaveIssue as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request.request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['project_save_failed'],
            str(error),
            error.details,
        )
    except ProjectDeleteIssue as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request.request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['project_delete_failed'],
            str(error),
            error.details,
        )
    except ProjectExportIssue as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request.request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['project_export_failed'],
            str(error),
            error.details,
        )
    except (ValidationError, ValueError) as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request.request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['validation'],
            'Invalid request payload',
            {'reason': str(error)},
        )
    except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
        return make_error_response(
            request.request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['internal'],
            'Unexpected internal error',
            {'reason': str(error)},
        )


==================================================
FILE: runtime_backend/app/services/project_catalog.py
==================================================

from __future__ import annotations

import shutil
from dataclasses import dataclass
from pathlib import Path

from runtime_backend.app.core.constants import PROJECT_STRUCTURE
from runtime_backend.app.core.settings import SETTINGS
from runtime_backend.app.db.bootstrap import connect
from runtime_backend.app.services.errors import ProjectCreateIssue, ProjectDeleteIssue, ProjectNotFoundIssue, ValidationIssue
from runtime_backend.app.utils.id_utils import make_project_id, slugify
from runtime_backend.app.utils.time_utils import utc_now_iso


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class PreparedProjectMetadata:
    project_id: str
    name: str
    slug: str
    root_path: Path
    project_file_path: Path
    created_at: str
    updated_at: str


def _to_summary(row) -> dict:
    return {
        'id': row['id'],
        'name': row['name'],
        'slug': row['slug'],
        'updatedAt': row['updated_at'],
        'lockedBy': None,
    }


def _serialize_project_yaml(project_id: str, project_name: str) -> str:
    escaped_name = project_name.replace('"', '\\"')
    lines = [
        f"kind: {PROJECT_STRUCTURE['kind']}",
        f"version: {PROJECT_STRUCTURE['version']}",
        'project:',
        f'  id: "{project_id}"',
        f'  name: "{escaped_name}"',
        '  description: ""',
        'modules:',
    ]

    for item in PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_display_names']:
        lines.append(f'  - {item}')

    lines.extend(
        [
            'paths:',
            f"  metagen: {PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_dirs'][0]}",
            f"  metalab: {PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_dirs'][1]}",
            f"  metaview: {PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_dirs'][2]}",
            f"  generated: {PROJECT_STRUCTURE['generated_dir']}",
            '',
        ]
    )
    return '\n'.join(lines)


def _next_available_slug(base_slug: str) -> str:
    with connect() as db:
        slug = base_slug
        suffix = 2
        while True:
            existing = db.execute('SELECT 1 FROM projects WHERE slug = ?', (slug,)).fetchone()
            if existing is None:
                return slug
            slug = f'{base_slug}-{suffix}'
            suffix += 1


def validate_project_name(name: str, *, field: str = 'name') -> str:
    normalized = str(name or '').strip()
    if not normalized:
        raise ValidationIssue('Project name is required', {'field': field})

    if len(normalized) > 120:
        raise ValidationIssue('Project name is too long', {'field': field, 'maxLength': 120})

    return normalized


def prepare_new_project_metadata(name: str, *, field: str = 'name') -> PreparedProjectMetadata:
    normalized_name = validate_project_name(name, field=field)
    base_slug = slugify(normalized_name)
    if not base_slug:
        raise ValidationIssue('Project name cannot be transformed into slug', {'field': field})

    slug = _next_available_slug(base_slug)
    project_id = make_project_id()
    now = utc_now_iso()
    project_root: Path = SETTINGS.workspace_projects_root / slug
    project_file_path = project_root / PROJECT_STRUCTURE['project_file_name']

    return PreparedProjectMetadata(
        project_id=project_id,
        name=normalized_name,
        slug=slug,
        root_path=project_root,
        project_file_path=project_file_path,
        created_at=now,
        updated_at=now,
    )


def register_prepared_project(metadata: PreparedProjectMetadata) -> dict:
    try:
        with connect() as db:
            db.execute(
                '''
                INSERT INTO projects(id, user_id, name, slug, root_path, project_file_path, created_at, updated_at)
                VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
                ''',
                (
                    metadata.project_id,
                    SETTINGS.default_user_id,
                    metadata.name,
                    metadata.slug,
                    metadata.root_path.as_posix(),
                    metadata.project_file_path.as_posix(),
                    metadata.created_at,
                    metadata.updated_at,
                ),
            )
            db.commit()
    except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
        raise ProjectCreateIssue(
            'Failed to save project record',
            {'slug': metadata.slug, 'reason': str(error)},
        ) from error

    return {
        'project': {
            'id': metadata.project_id,
            'name': metadata.name,
            'slug': metadata.slug,
            'updatedAt': metadata.updated_at,
            'lockedBy': None,
        }
    }


def list_projects() -> dict:
    with connect() as db:
        rows = db.execute(
            '''
            SELECT id, name, slug, updated_at
            FROM projects
            WHERE deleted_at IS NULL
            ORDER BY updated_at DESC, id DESC
            '''
        ).fetchall()

    return {'projects': [_to_summary(row) for row in rows]}


def create_project(payload: dict) -> dict:
    prepared = prepare_new_project_metadata(payload.get('name', ''), field='name')

    try:
        prepared.root_path.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=False)
        for folder in PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_dirs']:
            (prepared.root_path / folder).mkdir(parents=False, exist_ok=False)
        (prepared.root_path / PROJECT_STRUCTURE['generated_dir']).mkdir(parents=False, exist_ok=False)
        prepared.project_file_path.write_text(
            _serialize_project_yaml(prepared.project_id, prepared.name),
            encoding='utf-8',
        )
    except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
        if prepared.root_path.exists():
            shutil.rmtree(prepared.root_path, ignore_errors=True)
        raise ProjectCreateIssue(
            'Failed to create project files',
            {'slug': prepared.slug, 'reason': str(error)},
        ) from error

    try:
        return register_prepared_project(prepared)
    except ProjectCreateIssue:
        if prepared.root_path.exists():
            shutil.rmtree(prepared.root_path, ignore_errors=True)
        raise


def delete_project(payload: dict) -> dict:
    project_id = str(payload.get('projectId', '')).strip()
    if not project_id:
        raise ValidationIssue('Project id is required', {'field': 'projectId'})

    now = utc_now_iso()

    with connect() as db:
        row = db.execute(
            '''
            SELECT id, slug, root_path, deleted_at
            FROM projects
            WHERE id = ?
            ''',
            (project_id,),
        ).fetchone()

        if row is None:
            raise ProjectNotFoundIssue('Project not found', {'projectId': project_id})

        if row['deleted_at'] is not None:
            return {
                'projectId': project_id,
                'deleted': True,
                'alreadyDeleted': True,
            }

        project_root = Path(str(row['root_path']))
        deleted_root = SETTINGS.workspace_deleted_projects_root / f'{row["slug"]}__{project_id}'

        try:
            SETTINGS.workspace_deleted_projects_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
            if project_root.exists():
                if deleted_root.exists():
                    shutil.rmtree(deleted_root, ignore_errors=True)
                project_root.rename(deleted_root)
            db.execute(
                '''
                UPDATE projects
                SET deleted_at = ?, deleted_root_path = ?, updated_at = ?
                WHERE id = ?
                ''',
                (now, deleted_root.as_posix(), now, project_id),
            )
            db.commit()
        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
            raise ProjectDeleteIssue(
                'Failed to delete project',
                {'projectId': project_id, 'reason': str(error)},
            ) from error

    return {
        'projectId': project_id,
        'deleted': True,
        'alreadyDeleted': False,
    }


==================================================
FILE: runtime_backend/app/services/project_storage.py
==================================================

from __future__ import annotations

import shutil
import time
import zipfile
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any
from uuid import uuid4

import yaml

from runtime_backend.app.core.constants import PROJECT_STRUCTURE
from runtime_backend.app.core.constants import API_PROJECT_EXPORTS_ENDPOINT, PROJECT_EXPORT_ARTIFACT_MAX_AGE_SECONDS
from runtime_backend.app.core.settings import SETTINGS
from runtime_backend.app.db.bootstrap import connect
from runtime_backend.app.models.project_snapshot import (
    ProjectSnapshot,
    ProjectSnapshotDocument,
    ProjectSnapshotProject,
    SaveProjectAsPayload,
    SaveAllPayload,
)
from runtime_backend.app.services import project_catalog
from runtime_backend.app.services.errors import (
    ProjectCreateIssue,
    ProjectExportIssue,
    ProjectNotFoundIssue,
    ProjectOpenIssue,
    ProjectSaveIssue,
    ValidationIssue,
)
from runtime_backend.app.utils.time_utils import utc_now_iso


class ProjectStorageService:
    def __init__(self, db_connect=connect):
        self._db_connect = db_connect
        self._project_export_artifacts: dict[str, dict[str, str | float]] = {}

    def open_project_snapshot(self, payload: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
        project_id = str(payload.get('projectId', '')).strip()
        if not project_id:
            raise ValidationIssue('Project id is required', {'field': 'projectId'})

        project_row = self._load_project_metadata(project_id)
        project_root = Path(str(project_row['root_path']))
        project_file_path = Path(str(project_row['project_file_path']))
        self._verify_workspace_storage(
            project_id=project_id,
            project_slug=str(project_row['slug']),
            project_root=project_root,
            project_file_path=project_file_path,
        )

        if not project_root.exists():
            raise ProjectOpenIssue(
                'Project root path does not exist',
                {'projectId': project_id, 'rootPath': project_root.as_posix()},
            )

        raw = self._read_yaml_object(
            project_file_path,
            details={'projectId': project_id, 'projectFilePath': project_file_path.as_posix()},
        )

        snapshot = ProjectSnapshot(
            source=PROJECT_STRUCTURE['project_source_backend'],
            project=ProjectSnapshotProject(
                projectId=str(project_row['id']),
                name=str(project_row['name']),
                slug=str(project_row['slug']),
                updatedAt=str(project_row['updated_at']),
            ),
            raw=raw,
            documents={
                module_id: self._read_module_documents(
                    project_root=project_root,
                    project_id=project_id,
                    module_id=module_id,
                )
                for module_id in PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_dirs']
            },
        )

        return {'snapshot': snapshot.model_dump(by_alias=True)}

    def save_project_snapshot(self, payload: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
        try:
            save_payload = SaveAllPayload.model_validate(payload)
        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
            raise ValidationIssue('Invalid save payload', {'reason': str(error)}) from error

        project_id = save_payload.project_id
        if not project_id:
            raise ValidationIssue('Project id is required', {'field': 'projectId'})

        project_row = self._load_project_metadata(project_id)
        project_root = Path(str(project_row['root_path']))
        project_file_path = Path(str(project_row['project_file_path']))
        try:
            self._verify_workspace_storage(
                project_id=project_id,
                project_slug=str(project_row['slug']),
                project_root=project_root,
                project_file_path=project_file_path,
            )
        except ProjectOpenIssue as error:
            raise ProjectSaveIssue(str(error), error.details) from error

        if not project_root.exists():
            raise ProjectSaveIssue(
                'Project root path does not exist',
                {'projectId': project_id, 'rootPath': project_root.as_posix()},
            )

        raw = save_payload.project_snapshot.raw
        if not isinstance(raw, dict):
            raise ValidationIssue('Project snapshot raw is required', {'field': 'projectSnapshot.raw'})

        normalized_raw = self._normalize_raw_project(raw, project_id)
        normalized_documents = self._normalize_snapshot_documents(
            project_id=project_id,
            documents=save_payload.project_snapshot.documents,
        )

        staging_root = project_root / '.save-staging'
        backup_root = project_root / '.save-backup'
        promoted_modules: list[str] = []
        project_file_promoted = False
        project_name_for_catalog = str(project_row['name'])

        try:
            self._clear_path(staging_root)
            self._clear_path(backup_root)
            self._build_staging_snapshot(
                staging_root=staging_root,
                raw=normalized_raw,
                normalized_documents=normalized_documents,
            )

            for module_id in PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_dirs']:
                self._promote_module_dir(
                    project_root=project_root,
                    module_id=module_id,
                    staging_root=staging_root,
                    backup_root=backup_root,
                )
                promoted_modules.append(module_id)

            self._promote_project_file(
                project_file_path=project_file_path,
                staging_root=staging_root,
                backup_root=backup_root,
            )
            project_file_promoted = True
            project_name_for_catalog = self._extract_project_name(normalized_raw, default_name=project_name_for_catalog)
        except ValidationIssue:
            raise
        except ProjectNotFoundIssue:
            raise
        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
            rollback_errors = self._rollback_promoted_paths(
                project_root=project_root,
                project_file_path=project_file_path,
                backup_root=backup_root,
                promoted_modules=promoted_modules,
                project_file_promoted=project_file_promoted,
            )
            details = {'projectId': project_id, 'reason': str(error)}
            if rollback_errors:
                details['rollbackIssues'] = rollback_errors
            raise ProjectSaveIssue(
                'Failed to save project snapshot',
                details,
            ) from error
        finally:
            self._clear_path(staging_root)

        self._clear_path(backup_root)
        updated_at = self._touch_project_metadata(
            project_id=project_id,
            project_name=project_name_for_catalog,
        )
        project_meta = ProjectSnapshotProject(
            projectId=project_id,
            name=project_name_for_catalog,
            slug=str(project_row['slug']),
            updatedAt=updated_at,
        )
        return {
            'project': project_meta.model_dump(by_alias=True)
        }

    def save_project_snapshot_as(self, payload: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
        try:
            save_as_payload = SaveProjectAsPayload.model_validate(payload)
        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
            raise ValidationIssue('Invalid save-as payload', {'reason': str(error)}) from error

        source_project_id = str(save_as_payload.project_id or '').strip()
        if not source_project_id:
            raise ValidationIssue('Project id is required', {'field': 'projectId'})

        new_name = str(save_as_payload.new_name or '').strip()
        if not new_name:
            raise ValidationIssue('Project name is required', {'field': 'newName'})

        self._load_project_metadata(source_project_id)
        try:
            prepared = project_catalog.prepare_new_project_metadata(new_name, field='newName')
            raw = save_as_payload.project_snapshot.raw
            if not isinstance(raw, dict):
                raise ValidationIssue('Project snapshot raw is required', {'field': 'projectSnapshot.raw'})

            normalized_raw = self._normalize_raw_project(raw, prepared.project_id)
            normalized_raw['project']['id'] = prepared.project_id
            normalized_raw['project']['name'] = prepared.name

            normalized_documents = self._normalize_snapshot_documents(
                project_id=prepared.project_id,
                documents=save_as_payload.project_snapshot.documents,
            )

            return self._save_project_snapshot_as_new_project(
                source_project_id=source_project_id,
                prepared=prepared,
                normalized_raw=normalized_raw,
                normalized_documents=normalized_documents,
            )
        except ProjectNotFoundIssue:
            raise
        except ProjectCreateIssue:
            raise
        except ValidationIssue:
            raise
        except ProjectSaveIssue:
            raise
        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
            raise ProjectSaveIssue(
                'Failed to save project snapshot as new project',
                {'projectId': source_project_id, 'reason': str(error)},
            ) from error

    def _load_project_metadata(self, project_id: str):
        with self._db_connect() as db:
            row = db.execute(
                '''
                SELECT id, name, slug, root_path, project_file_path, updated_at
                FROM projects
                WHERE id = ? AND deleted_at IS NULL
                ''',
                (project_id,),
            ).fetchone()

        if row is None:
            raise ProjectNotFoundIssue('Project not found', {'projectId': project_id})

        return row

    def _save_project_snapshot_as_new_project(
        self,
        *,
        source_project_id: str,
        prepared: project_catalog.PreparedProjectMetadata,
        normalized_raw: dict[str, Any],
        normalized_documents: dict[str, list[tuple[str, dict[str, Any]]]],
    ) -> dict[str, Any]:
        project_root = prepared.root_path
        project_file_path = prepared.project_file_path
        staging_root = project_root / '.save-staging'
        backup_root = project_root / '.save-backup'
        promoted_modules: list[str] = []
        project_file_promoted = False
        created_project_root = False

        try:
            project_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=False)
            created_project_root = True
            self._clear_path(staging_root)
            self._clear_path(backup_root)
            self._build_staging_snapshot(
                staging_root=staging_root,
                raw=normalized_raw,
                normalized_documents=normalized_documents,
            )

            for module_id in PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_dirs']:
                self._promote_module_dir(
                    project_root=project_root,
                    module_id=module_id,
                    staging_root=staging_root,
                    backup_root=backup_root,
                )
                promoted_modules.append(module_id)

            self._promote_project_file(
                project_file_path=project_file_path,
                staging_root=staging_root,
                backup_root=backup_root,
            )
            project_file_promoted = True
            (project_root / PROJECT_STRUCTURE['generated_dir']).mkdir(parents=False, exist_ok=False)
        except ValidationIssue:
            raise
        except ProjectNotFoundIssue:
            raise
        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
            rollback_errors = self._rollback_promoted_paths(
                project_root=project_root,
                project_file_path=project_file_path,
                backup_root=backup_root,
                promoted_modules=promoted_modules,
                project_file_promoted=project_file_promoted,
            )
            if created_project_root:
                self._clear_path(project_root)
            details = {'projectId': source_project_id, 'reason': str(error)}
            if rollback_errors:
                details['rollbackIssues'] = rollback_errors
            raise ProjectSaveIssue(
                'Failed to save project snapshot as new project',
                details,
            ) from error
        finally:
            self._clear_path(staging_root)
            self._clear_path(backup_root)

        try:
            project_catalog.register_prepared_project(prepared)
        except ProjectCreateIssue as error:
            if created_project_root:
                self._clear_path(project_root)
            raise ProjectCreateIssue(
                str(error),
                {'projectId': source_project_id, **(error.details or {})},
            ) from error
        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
            if created_project_root:
                self._clear_path(project_root)
            raise ProjectCreateIssue(
                'Failed to save project record',
                {'projectId': source_project_id, 'slug': prepared.slug, 'reason': str(error)},
            ) from error

        project_meta = ProjectSnapshotProject(
            projectId=prepared.project_id,
            name=prepared.name,
            slug=prepared.slug,
            updatedAt=prepared.updated_at,
        )
        return {'project': project_meta.model_dump(by_alias=True)}

    def export_project_archive(self, payload: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
        self._prune_project_export_artifacts()

        project_id = str(payload.get('projectId', '')).strip()
        if not project_id:
            raise ValidationIssue('Project id is required', {'field': 'projectId'})

        project_row = self._load_project_metadata(project_id)
        project_slug = str(project_row['slug'])
        project_root = Path(str(project_row['root_path']))
        project_file_path = Path(str(project_row['project_file_path']))
        try:
            self._verify_workspace_storage(
                project_id=project_id,
                project_slug=project_slug,
                project_root=project_root,
                project_file_path=project_file_path,
            )
        except ProjectOpenIssue as error:
            raise ProjectExportIssue(str(error), error.details) from error

        if not project_root.exists():
            raise ProjectExportIssue(
                'Project root path does not exist',
                {'projectId': project_id, 'rootPath': project_root.as_posix()},
            )

        export_token = f'export_{uuid4().hex}'
        archive_file_name = f'{project_slug}.zip'
        export_root = SETTINGS.workspace_project_exports_root
        export_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        archive_path = export_root / f'{export_token}.zip'

        try:
            if archive_path.exists():
                archive_path.unlink(missing_ok=True)

            with zipfile.ZipFile(archive_path, mode='w', compression=zipfile.ZIP_DEFLATED) as archive:
                archive.write(project_file_path, arcname=PROJECT_STRUCTURE['project_file_name'])
                self._write_project_dir_to_archive(archive, project_root, PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_dirs'])
                self._write_project_dir_to_archive(archive, project_root, [PROJECT_STRUCTURE['generated_dir']])
        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
            archive_path.unlink(missing_ok=True)
            raise ProjectExportIssue(
                'Failed to export project archive',
                {'projectId': project_id, 'reason': str(error)},
            ) from error

        self._project_export_artifacts[export_token] = {
            'path': archive_path.as_posix(),
            'fileName': archive_file_name,
            'projectId': project_id,
            'createdAt': time.time(),
        }
        return {
            'exportToken': export_token,
            'downloadUrl': f'{API_PROJECT_EXPORTS_ENDPOINT}/{export_token}',
            'fileName': archive_file_name,
        }

    def consume_project_export_artifact(self, export_token: str) -> dict[str, str] | None:
        self._prune_project_export_artifacts()

        normalized_token = str(export_token or '').strip()
        if not normalized_token:
            return None
        artifact = self._project_export_artifacts.pop(normalized_token, None)
        if artifact is None:
            return None

        artifact_path = Path(str(artifact['path']))
        if not artifact_path.exists() or not artifact_path.is_file():
            return None

        return {
            'path': str(artifact['path']),
            'fileName': str(artifact['fileName']),
            'projectId': str(artifact['projectId']),
        }

    def _prune_project_export_artifacts(self) -> None:
        now = time.time()
        max_age_seconds = PROJECT_EXPORT_ARTIFACT_MAX_AGE_SECONDS
        export_root = SETTINGS.workspace_project_exports_root
        export_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

        expired_tokens: list[str] = []
        for token, artifact in self._project_export_artifacts.items():
            created_at = float(artifact.get('createdAt') or 0.0)
            if created_at > 0 and now - created_at <= max_age_seconds:
                continue

            artifact_path = Path(str(artifact.get('path', '')))
            artifact_path.unlink(missing_ok=True)
            expired_tokens.append(token)

        for token in expired_tokens:
            self._project_export_artifacts.pop(token, None)

        for artifact_path in export_root.glob('*.zip'):
            try:
                if now - artifact_path.stat().st_mtime > max_age_seconds:
                    artifact_path.unlink(missing_ok=True)
            except OSError:
                continue

    @staticmethod
    def _verify_workspace_storage(
        *,
        project_id: str,
        project_slug: str,
        project_root: Path,
        project_file_path: Path,
    ) -> None:
        workspace_root = SETTINGS.workspace_projects_root.resolve()
        expected_project_root = (workspace_root / project_slug).resolve()
        resolved_project_root = project_root.resolve()

        if resolved_project_root != expected_project_root:
            raise ProjectOpenIssue(
                'Project root path is inconsistent with workspace storage',
                {
                    'projectId': project_id,
                    'rootPath': project_root.as_posix(),
                    'workspaceProjectsRoot': workspace_root.as_posix(),
                    'expectedRootPath': expected_project_root.as_posix(),
                },
            )

        expected_project_file = (expected_project_root / PROJECT_STRUCTURE['project_file_name']).resolve()
        resolved_project_file = project_file_path.resolve()

        if resolved_project_file != expected_project_file:
            raise ProjectOpenIssue(
                'Project file path is inconsistent with workspace storage',
                {
                    'projectId': project_id,
                    'projectFilePath': project_file_path.as_posix(),
                    'expectedProjectFilePath': expected_project_file.as_posix(),
                },
            )

    def _read_module_documents(self, project_root: Path, project_id: str, module_id: str) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
        module_path = project_root / module_id
        if not module_path.exists() or not module_path.is_dir():
            return []

        records: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
        for file_path in sorted(module_path.iterdir(), key=lambda entry: entry.name.lower()):
            if not file_path.is_file():
                continue
            if file_path.suffix.lower() not in PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_file_extensions']:
                continue

            document = self._read_yaml_object(
                file_path,
                details={
                    'projectId': project_id,
                    'moduleId': module_id,
                    'path': file_path.as_posix(),
                },
            )
            records.append(
                ProjectSnapshotDocument(
                    moduleId=module_id,
                    path=f"backend://{project_id}/{module_id}/{file_path.name}",
                    document=document,
                ).model_dump(by_alias=True)
            )

        return records

    @staticmethod
    def _extract_project_name(raw: dict[str, Any], default_name: str) -> str:
        project_node = raw.get('project')
        if not isinstance(project_node, dict):
            return default_name

        value = str(project_node.get('name', '')).strip()
        return value or default_name

    @staticmethod
    def _normalize_raw_project(raw: dict[str, Any], project_id: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
        cloned = yaml.safe_load(yaml.safe_dump(raw, sort_keys=False, allow_unicode=True))
        if not isinstance(cloned, dict):
            raise ValidationIssue('Project snapshot raw must be an object', {'field': 'projectSnapshot.raw'})

        project = cloned.get('project')
        if not isinstance(project, dict):
            project = {}

        project['id'] = str(project.get('id') or project_id)
        project['name'] = str(project.get('name', '') or 'project').strip() or 'project'
        project['description'] = str(project.get('description', '') or '')
        cloned['project'] = project
        return cloned

    def _normalize_snapshot_documents(
        self,
        *,
        project_id: str,
        documents: dict[str, list[ProjectSnapshotDocument]],
    ) -> dict[str, list[tuple[str, dict[str, Any]]]]:
        normalized: dict[str, list[tuple[str, dict[str, Any]]]] = {}

        for module_id in PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_dirs']:
            module_entries = documents.get(module_id, [])
            if not isinstance(module_entries, list):
                raise ValidationIssue('Project snapshot documents must be grouped by module', {'moduleId': module_id})

            occupied_file_names: set[str] = set()
            module_records: list[tuple[str, dict[str, Any]]] = []
            for index, entry in enumerate(module_entries):
                if not isinstance(entry.document, dict):
                    raise ValidationIssue(
                        'Project snapshot document payload must be an object',
                        {'moduleId': module_id, 'index': index},
                    )

                file_name = self._resolve_document_file_name(
                    project_id=project_id,
                    module_id=module_id,
                    index=index,
                    entry=entry,
                )
                normalized_file_name = file_name.lower()
                if normalized_file_name in occupied_file_names:
                    raise ValidationIssue(
                        'Filename collision detected in project snapshot',
                        {'moduleId': module_id, 'fileName': file_name},
                    )

                occupied_file_names.add(normalized_file_name)
                module_records.append((file_name, entry.document))

            normalized[module_id] = module_records

        return normalized

    @staticmethod
    def _resolve_document_file_name(
        *,
        project_id: str,
        module_id: str,
        index: int,
        entry: ProjectSnapshotDocument,
    ) -> str:
        path_value = str(entry.path or '').strip()
        name = Path(path_value).name
        if not name:
            name = f'{module_id}-{index + 1}.yaml'
        if '/' in name or '\\' in name:
            raise ValidationIssue(
                'Document path must resolve to a single file name',
                {'projectId': project_id, 'moduleId': module_id, 'path': path_value},
            )
        if Path(name).suffix.lower() not in PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_file_extensions']:
            name = f'{Path(name).stem}.yaml'

        safe_name = Path(name).name.strip()
        if not safe_name:
            safe_name = f'{module_id}-{index + 1}.yaml'
        return safe_name

    def _build_staging_snapshot(
        self,
        *,
        staging_root: Path,
        raw: dict[str, Any],
        normalized_documents: dict[str, list[tuple[str, dict[str, Any]]]],
    ) -> None:
        staging_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=False)

        for module_id in PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_dirs']:
            (staging_root / module_id).mkdir(parents=False, exist_ok=False)

        for module_id, records in normalized_documents.items():
            module_root = staging_root / module_id
            for file_name, document in records:
                self._write_yaml_object(module_root / file_name, document)

        self._write_yaml_object(staging_root / PROJECT_STRUCTURE['project_file_name'], raw)

    @staticmethod
    def _clear_path(target_path: Path) -> None:
        if not target_path.exists():
            return
        if target_path.is_dir():
            shutil.rmtree(target_path, ignore_errors=True)
            return
        target_path.unlink(missing_ok=True)

    def _promote_module_dir(
        self,
        *,
        project_root: Path,
        module_id: str,
        staging_root: Path,
        backup_root: Path,
    ) -> None:
        current_path = project_root / module_id
        staged_path = staging_root / module_id
        backup_path = backup_root / module_id

        backup_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        self._clear_path(backup_path)
        if current_path.exists():
            current_path.rename(backup_path)
        staged_path.rename(current_path)

    def _promote_project_file(
        self,
        *,
        project_file_path: Path,
        staging_root: Path,
        backup_root: Path,
    ) -> None:
        staged_project_file = staging_root / PROJECT_STRUCTURE['project_file_name']
        backup_project_file = backup_root / PROJECT_STRUCTURE['project_file_name']

        backup_project_file.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        self._clear_path(backup_project_file)
        if project_file_path.exists():
            project_file_path.rename(backup_project_file)
        staged_project_file.rename(project_file_path)

    def _rollback_promoted_paths(
        self,
        *,
        project_root: Path,
        project_file_path: Path,
        backup_root: Path,
        promoted_modules: list[str],
        project_file_promoted: bool,
    ) -> list[str]:
        rollback_errors: list[str] = []

        if project_file_promoted:
            backup_project_file = backup_root / PROJECT_STRUCTURE['project_file_name']
            try:
                self._clear_path(project_file_path)
                if backup_project_file.exists():
                    backup_project_file.rename(project_file_path)
            except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
                rollback_errors.append(f'project.yaml rollback failed: {error}')

        for module_id in reversed(promoted_modules):
            current_path = project_root / module_id
            backup_path = backup_root / module_id
            try:
                self._clear_path(current_path)
                if backup_path.exists():
                    backup_path.rename(current_path)
            except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
                rollback_errors.append(f'{module_id} rollback failed: {error}')

        return rollback_errors

    def _touch_project_metadata(self, *, project_id: str, project_name: str) -> str:
        updated_at = utc_now_iso()
        with self._db_connect() as db:
            db.execute(
                'UPDATE projects SET name = ?, updated_at = ? WHERE id = ?',
                (project_name, updated_at, project_id),
            )
            db.commit()

        return updated_at

    @staticmethod
    def _write_project_dir_to_archive(
        archive: zipfile.ZipFile,
        project_root: Path,
        folder_names: list[str],
    ) -> None:
        for folder_name in folder_names:
            folder_root = project_root / folder_name
            if not folder_root.exists() or not folder_root.is_dir():
                continue

            archive.writestr(f'{folder_name}/', b'')
            for file_path in sorted(folder_root.rglob('*')):
                if file_path.is_dir():
                    continue
                relative_path = file_path.relative_to(project_root).as_posix()
                archive.write(file_path, arcname=relative_path)

    @staticmethod
    def _read_yaml_object(path: Path, details: dict[str, Any] | None = None) -> dict[str, Any]:
        if not path.exists():
            raise ProjectOpenIssue('YAML file does not exist', {**(details or {}), 'path': path.as_posix()})

        try:
            parsed = yaml.safe_load(path.read_text(encoding='utf-8'))
        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
            raise ProjectOpenIssue(
                'Failed to read YAML file',
                {**(details or {}), 'path': path.as_posix(), 'reason': str(error)},
            ) from error

        if not isinstance(parsed, dict):
            raise ProjectOpenIssue(
                'YAML root must be an object',
                {**(details or {}), 'path': path.as_posix()},
            )

        return parsed

    @staticmethod
    def _write_yaml_object(path: Path, payload: dict[str, Any]) -> None:
        path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        path.write_text(
            yaml.safe_dump(payload, sort_keys=False, allow_unicode=True),
            encoding='utf-8',
        )

==================================================

﻿import re
import uuid


NON_ALNUM = re.compile(r'[^a-z0-9]+')
TRIM_DASH = re.compile(r'^-+|-+$')


def make_project_id() -> str:
    return f"proj_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:12]}"


def slugify(value: str) -> str:
    normalized = NON_ALNUM.sub('-', value.strip().lower())
    return TRIM_DASH.sub('', normalized)


==================================================
FILE: runtime_backend/app/utils/time_utils.py
==================================================

﻿from datetime import datetime, timezone


def utc_now_iso() -> str:
    return datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(timespec='seconds').replace('+00:00', 'Z')

from dataclasses import replace

@pytest.fixture()
def runtime_env(tmp_path, monkeypatch):
    data_root = tmp_path / 'runtime_data'
    test_settings = replace(
        SETTINGS,
        data_root=data_root,
        sqlite_path=data_root / 'platform.db',
        workspace_projects_root=data_root / 'workspace' / 'projects',
        workspace_deleted_projects_root=data_root / 'workspace' / 'deleted_projects',
        workspace_project_exports_root=data_root / 'workspace' / 'exports',
    )

    monkeypatch.setattr(db_bootstrap, 'SETTINGS', test_settings)
    monkeypatch.setattr(project_catalog, 'SETTINGS', test_settings)
    monkeypatch.setattr(project_storage, 'SETTINGS', test_settings)
    command_dispatcher.project_storage_service._project_export_artifacts.clear()

    db_bootstrap.bootstrap_storage()
    return test_settings

def test_create_project_success_and_fs_structure(runtime_env):
    client = TestClient(app)

    create_response = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-create',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'createProject',
            'payload': {'name': 'Alpha Plant'},
        },
    )
    assert create_response.status_code == 200
    create_body = create_response.json()
    assert create_body['ok'] is True

    project = create_body['result']['project']
    assert project['name'] == 'Alpha Plant'
    assert project['slug'] == 'alpha-plant'
    assert project['lockedBy'] is None

    root = runtime_env.workspace_projects_root / project['slug']
    assert root.exists()
    assert (root / 'project.yaml').exists()
    assert (root / 'metagen').exists()
    assert (root / 'metalab').exists()
    assert (root / 'metaview').exists()
    assert (root / 'generated').exists()

    project_yaml = (root / 'project.yaml').read_text(encoding='utf-8')
    assert 'kind: metaplatform.project' in project_yaml
    assert 'modules:' in project_yaml
    assert 'MetaGen' in project_yaml

    list_response = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-list-after-create',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'listProjects',
            'payload': {},
        },
    )
    body = list_response.json()
    assert body['ok'] is True
    assert len(body['result']['projects']) == 1
    assert body['result']['projects'][0]['slug'] == 'alpha-plant'

def test_open_project_success_returns_snapshot_with_raw_and_documents(runtime_env):
    client = TestClient(app)
    created = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-create-openable',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'createProject',
            'payload': {'name': 'Backend Open'},
        },
    ).json()
    project = created['result']['project']

    project_root = runtime_env.workspace_projects_root / project['slug']
    metagen_file = project_root / 'metagen' / 'pump.yaml'
    metalab_file = project_root / 'metalab' / 'startup.yaml'
    metaview_file = project_root / 'metaview' / 'main.yaml'

    metagen_file.write_text(
        yaml.safe_dump(
            {
                'kind': 'metagen.component',
                'component': {'id': 'pump', 'name': 'Pump'},
            },
            sort_keys=False,
            allow_unicode=True,
        ),
        encoding='utf-8',
    )
    metalab_file.write_text(
        yaml.safe_dump(
            {
                'kind': 'metalab.scenario',
                'scenario': {'id': 'startup', 'name': 'Startup'},
            },
            sort_keys=False,
            allow_unicode=True,
        ),
        encoding='utf-8',
    )
    metaview_file.write_text(
        yaml.safe_dump(
            {
                'kind': 'metaview.screen',
                'screen': {'id': 'main', 'name': 'Main'},
            },
            sort_keys=False,
            allow_unicode=True,
        ),
        encoding='utf-8',
    )

    opened = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-open-success',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'openProject',
            'payload': {'projectId': project['id']},
        },
    ).json()

    assert opened['ok'] is True
    snapshot = opened['result']['snapshot']
    assert snapshot['source'] == 'backend'
    assert snapshot['project']['projectId'] == project['id']
    assert snapshot['project']['name'] == project['name']
    assert snapshot['project']['slug'] == project['slug']
    assert snapshot['raw']['kind'] == 'metaplatform.project'
    assert snapshot['raw']['project']['id'] == project['id']
    assert len(snapshot['documents']['metagen']) == 1
    assert len(snapshot['documents']['metalab']) == 1
    assert len(snapshot['documents']['metaview']) == 1
    assert snapshot['documents']['metagen'][0]['path'].startswith(f"backend://{project['id']}/metagen/")
    assert snapshot['documents']['metagen'][0]['document']['component']['name'] == 'Pump'

def test_open_project_missing_root_path_returns_project_open_failed(runtime_env):
    client = TestClient(app)
    created = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-create-missing-root',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'createProject',
            'payload': {'name': 'Missing Root'},
        },
    ).json()
    project = created['result']['project']
    project_root = runtime_env.workspace_projects_root / project['slug']

    for item in project_root.rglob('*'):
        if item.is_file():
            item.unlink()
    for directory in sorted([entry for entry in project_root.rglob('*') if entry.is_dir()], reverse=True):
        directory.rmdir()
    project_root.rmdir()

    response = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-open-missing-root',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'openProject',
            'payload': {'projectId': project['id']},
        },
    )

    body = response.json()
    assert body['ok'] is False
    assert body['error']['code'] == 'PROJECT_OPEN_FAILED'
    assert body['error']['details']['projectId'] == project['id']

    client = TestClient(app)
    created = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-create-storage-mismatch',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'createProject',
            'payload': {'name': 'Storage Mismatch'},
        },
    ).json()
    project = created['result']['project']

    bad_root = (runtime_env.data_root / 'outside-root').as_posix()
    bad_project_file = (runtime_env.data_root / 'outside-root' / 'project.yaml').as_posix()

    with db_bootstrap.connect() as db:
        db.execute(
            'UPDATE projects SET root_path = ?, project_file_path = ? WHERE id = ?',
            (bad_root, bad_project_file, project['id']),
        )
        db.commit()

    response = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-open-storage-mismatch',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'openProject',
            'payload': {'projectId': project['id']},
        },
    )

    body = response.json()
    assert body['ok'] is False
    assert body['error']['code'] == 'PROJECT_OPEN_FAILED'
    assert body['error']['details']['projectId'] == project['id']


def test_delete_project_success_moves_storage_and_marks_deleted(runtime_env):
    client = TestClient(app)
    created = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-create-delete-success',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'createProject',
            'payload': {'name': 'Delete Success'},
        },
    ).json()
    project = created['result']['project']
    project_root = runtime_env.workspace_projects_root / project['slug']
    project_file_before = (project_root / 'project.yaml').read_text(encoding='utf-8')

    response = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-delete-success',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'deleteProject',
            'payload': {'projectId': project['id']},
        },
    )
    body = response.json()
    assert body['ok'] is True
    assert body['result']['projectId'] == project['id']
    assert body['result']['deleted'] is True
    assert body['result']['alreadyDeleted'] is False

    assert not project_root.exists()
    deleted_root = runtime_env.workspace_deleted_projects_root / f"{project['slug']}__{project['id']}"
    assert deleted_root.exists()
    assert (deleted_root / 'project.yaml').read_text(encoding='utf-8') == project_file_before

    with db_bootstrap.connect() as db:
        row = db.execute(
            'SELECT deleted_at, deleted_root_path FROM projects WHERE id = ?',
            (project['id'],),
        ).fetchone()
    assert row is not None
    assert row['deleted_at'] is not None
    assert row['deleted_root_path'] == deleted_root.as_posix()

def test_deleted_project_is_hidden_from_list_and_open_save_fail_as_not_found(runtime_env):
    client = TestClient(app)
    created = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-create-delete-hide',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'createProject',
            'payload': {'name': 'Delete Hide'},
        },
    ).json()
    project = created['result']['project']

    delete_response = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-delete-hide',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'deleteProject',
            'payload': {'projectId': project['id']},
        },
    ).json()
    assert delete_response['ok'] is True

    list_response = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-list-after-delete-hide',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'listProjects',
            'payload': {},
        },
    ).json()
    assert list_response['ok'] is True
    listed_ids = [item['id'] for item in list_response['result']['projects']]
    assert project['id'] not in listed_ids

    open_response = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-open-after-delete-hide',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'openProject',
            'payload': {'projectId': project['id']},
        },
    ).json()
    assert open_response['ok'] is False
    assert open_response['error']['code'] == 'PROJECT_NOT_FOUND'
    assert open_response['error']['details']['projectId'] == project['id']

    save_response = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-save-after-delete-hide',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'saveAll',
            'payload': {
                'projectId': project['id'],
                'projectSnapshot': {
                    'raw': {'project': {'id': project['id'], 'name': 'deleted'}},
                    'documents': {'metagen': [], 'metalab': [], 'metaview': []},
                },
            },
        },
    ).json()
    assert save_response['ok'] is False
    assert save_response['error']['code'] == 'PROJECT_NOT_FOUND'
    assert save_response['error']['details']['projectId'] == project['id']


def test_delete_project_repeated_call_is_idempotent_success(runtime_env):
    client = TestClient(app)
    created = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-create-delete-repeat',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'createProject',
            'payload': {'name': 'Delete Repeat'},
        },
    ).json()
    project = created['result']['project']

    first = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-delete-repeat-first',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'deleteProject',
            'payload': {'projectId': project['id']},
        },
    ).json()
    assert first['ok'] is True
    assert first['result']['alreadyDeleted'] is False

    second = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-delete-repeat-second',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'deleteProject',
            'payload': {'projectId': project['id']},
        },
    ).json()
    assert second['ok'] is True
    assert second['result']['projectId'] == project['id']
    assert second['result']['deleted'] is True
    assert second['result']['alreadyDeleted'] is True


def test_save_all_success_updates_canonical_project_files(runtime_env):
    client = TestClient(app)
    created = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-create-saveall',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'createProject',
            'payload': {'name': 'Save All Project'},
        },
    ).json()
    project = created['result']['project']

    project_root = runtime_env.workspace_projects_root / project['slug']
    generated_file = project_root / 'generated' / 'keep.txt'
    generated_file.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    generated_file.write_text('keep-generated', encoding='utf-8')

    save_response = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-save-success',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'saveAll',
            'payload': {
                'projectId': project['id'],
                'projectSnapshot': {
                    'raw': {
                        'kind': 'metaplatform.project',
                        'version': 1,
                        'project': {
                            'id': project['id'],
                            'name': 'Save All Updated',
                            'description': 'updated',
                        },
                        'modules': ['MetaGen', 'MetaLab', 'MetaView'],
                        'paths': {
                            'metagen': 'metagen',
                            'metalab': 'metalab',
                            'metaview': 'metaview',
                            'generated': 'generated',
                        },
                    },
                    'documents': {
                        'metagen': [
                            {
                                'moduleId': 'metagen',
                                'path': f"backend://{project['id']}/metagen/pump.yaml",
                                'document': {
                                    'kind': 'metagen.component',
                                    'component': {'id': 'pump', 'name': 'Pump'},
                                },
                            }
                        ],
                        'metalab': [
                            {
                                'moduleId': 'metalab',
                                'path': f"backend://{project['id']}/metalab/startup.yaml",
                                'document': {
                                    'kind': 'metalab.scenario',
                                    'scenario': {'id': 'startup', 'name': 'Startup'},
                                },
                            }
                        ],
                        'metaview': [
                            {
                                'moduleId': 'metaview',
                                'path': f"backend://{project['id']}/metaview/main.yaml",
                                'document': {
                                    'kind': 'metaview.screen',
                                    'screen': {'id': 'main', 'name': 'Main'},
                                },
                            }
                        ],
                    },
                },
            },
        },
    )

    body = save_response.json()
    assert body['ok'] is True
    assert body['result']['project']['projectId'] == project['id']
    assert body['result']['project']['name'] == 'Save All Updated'
    assert 'id' not in body['result']['project']

    project_yaml = yaml.safe_load((project_root / 'project.yaml').read_text(encoding='utf-8'))
    metagen_yaml = yaml.safe_load((project_root / 'metagen' / 'pump.yaml').read_text(encoding='utf-8'))
    metalab_yaml = yaml.safe_load((project_root / 'metalab' / 'startup.yaml').read_text(encoding='utf-8'))
    metaview_yaml = yaml.safe_load((project_root / 'metaview' / 'main.yaml').read_text(encoding='utf-8'))

    assert project_yaml['project']['name'] == 'Save All Updated'
    assert metagen_yaml['component']['name'] == 'Pump'
    assert metalab_yaml['scenario']['name'] == 'Startup'
    assert metaview_yaml['screen']['name'] == 'Main'
    assert generated_file.read_text(encoding='utf-8') == 'keep-generated'

def test_save_all_failure_after_partial_promote_rolls_back_canonical_state(runtime_env, monkeypatch):
    client = TestClient(app)
    created = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-create-save-rollback',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'createProject',
            'payload': {'name': 'Rollback Guard'},
        },
    ).json()
    project = created['result']['project']
    project_root = runtime_env.workspace_projects_root / project['slug']

    metagen_file = project_root / 'metagen' / 'legacy.yaml'
    metagen_file.write_text(
        yaml.safe_dump(
            {
                'kind': 'metagen.component',
                'component': {'id': 'legacy', 'name': 'Legacy', 'description': 'before-failure'},
            },
            sort_keys=False,
            allow_unicode=True,
        ),
        encoding='utf-8',
    )

    def raise_promote_failure(*_args, **_kwargs):
        raise OSError('Injected project file promote failure')

    monkeypatch.setattr(project_storage.ProjectStorageService, '_promote_project_file', raise_promote_failure)

    response = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-save-rollback',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'saveAll',
            'payload': {
                'projectId': project['id'],
                'projectSnapshot': {
                    'raw': {'project': {'id': project['id'], 'name': 'Should Not Persist'}},
                    'documents': {
                        'metagen': [
                            {
                                'moduleId': 'metagen',
                                'path': f"backend://{project['id']}/metagen/legacy.yaml",
                                'document': {
                                    'kind': 'metagen.component',
                                    'component': {'id': 'legacy', 'name': 'Legacy', 'description': 'after-failure'},
                                },
                            }
                        ],
                        'metalab': [],
                        'metaview': [],
                    },
                },
            },
        },
    )

    body = response.json()
    assert body['ok'] is False
    assert body['error']['code'] == 'PROJECT_SAVE_FAILED'
    assert body['error']['details']['projectId'] == project['id']

    restored_metagen = yaml.safe_load(metagen_file.read_text(encoding='utf-8'))
    assert restored_metagen['component']['description'] == 'before-failure'

    restored_project_yaml = yaml.safe_load((project_root / 'project.yaml').read_text(encoding='utf-8'))
    assert restored_project_yaml['project']['name'] == project['name']

    list_response = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-list-after-rollback',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'listProjects',
            'payload': {},
        },
    ).json()
    assert list_response['ok'] is True
    assert list_response['result']['projects'][0]['name'] == project['name']

    assert not (project_root / '.save-staging').exists()


def test_save_project_as_success_creates_new_project_and_preserves_snapshot(runtime_env):
    client = TestClient(app)
    created = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-create-save-as-src',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'createProject',
            'payload': {'name': 'Source Project'},
        },
    ).json()
    source_project = created['result']['project']

    source_root = runtime_env.workspace_projects_root / source_project['slug']
    (source_root / 'generated' / 'keep.txt').write_text('generated-keep', encoding='utf-8')

    save_as_response = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-save-as-success',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'saveProjectAs',
            'payload': {
                'projectId': source_project['id'],
                'newName': 'Cloned Project',
                'projectSnapshot': {
                    'raw': {
                        'kind': 'metaplatform.project',
                        'version': 1,
                        'project': {
                            'id': source_project['id'],
                            'name': 'Source Project',
                            'description': 'cloned',
                        },
                        'modules': ['MetaGen', 'MetaLab', 'MetaView'],
                        'paths': {
                            'metagen': 'metagen',
                            'metalab': 'metalab',
                            'metaview': 'metaview',
                            'generated': 'generated',
                        },
                    },
                    'documents': {
                        'metagen': [
                            {
                                'moduleId': 'metagen',
                                'path': f"backend://{source_project['id']}/metagen/pump.yaml",
                                'document': {
                                    'kind': 'metagen.component',
                                    'component': {'id': 'pump', 'name': 'Pump'},
                                },
                            }
                        ],
                        'metalab': [],
                        'metaview': [],
                    },
                },
            },
        },
    )

    body = save_as_response.json()
    assert body['ok'] is True
    created_project = body['result']['project']
    assert created_project['projectId'] != source_project['id']
    assert created_project['name'] == 'Cloned Project'

    list_response = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-list-save-as',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'listProjects',
            'payload': {},
        },
    ).json()
    assert list_response['ok'] is True
    assert len(list_response['result']['projects']) == 2

    new_summary = next(
        project
        for project in list_response['result']['projects']
        if project['id'] == created_project['projectId']
    )
    new_root = runtime_env.workspace_projects_root / new_summary['slug']
    assert new_root.exists()
    assert (new_root / 'metagen').exists()
    assert (new_root / 'metalab').exists()
    assert (new_root / 'metaview').exists()
    assert (new_root / 'generated').exists()

    new_project_yaml = yaml.safe_load((new_root / 'project.yaml').read_text(encoding='utf-8'))
    assert new_project_yaml['project']['id'] == created_project['projectId']
    assert new_project_yaml['project']['name'] == 'Cloned Project'

    opened = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-open-save-as-result',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'openProject',
            'payload': {'projectId': created_project['projectId']},
        },
    ).json()
    assert opened['ok'] is True
    assert opened['result']['snapshot']['project']['projectId'] == created_project['projectId']
    assert opened['result']['snapshot']['project']['name'] == 'Cloned Project'
    assert opened['result']['snapshot']['documents']['metagen'][0]['document']['component']['name'] == 'Pump'
    assert opened['result']['snapshot']['documents']['metagen'][0]['path'].startswith(
        f"backend://{created_project['projectId']}/metagen/"
    )

def test_save_project_as_write_failure_returns_project_save_failed_and_rolls_back_new_project(runtime_env, monkeypatch):
    client = TestClient(app)
    created = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-create-save-as-write-fail-src',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'createProject',
            'payload': {'name': 'Write Failure Source'},
        },
    ).json()
    source_project = created['result']['project']
    source_project_id = source_project['id']
    source_root = runtime_env.workspace_projects_root / source_project['slug']
    source_project_yaml_before = (source_root / 'project.yaml').read_text(encoding='utf-8')

    def raise_write_failure(*_args, **_kwargs):
        raise OSError('Injected write failure for save-as')

    monkeypatch.setattr(project_storage.ProjectStorageService, '_write_yaml_object', staticmethod(raise_write_failure))

    response = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-save-as-write-fail',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'saveProjectAs',
            'payload': {
                'projectId': source_project_id,
                'newName': 'Write Failure Copy',
                'projectSnapshot': {
                    'raw': {'project': {'id': source_project_id, 'name': 'Write Failure Copy'}},
                    'documents': {'metagen': [], 'metalab': [], 'metaview': []},
                },
            },
        },
    )

    body = response.json()
    assert body['ok'] is False
    assert body['error']['code'] == 'PROJECT_SAVE_FAILED'
    assert body['error']['details']['projectId'] == source_project_id

    list_response = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-list-after-save-as-fail',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'listProjects',
            'payload': {},
        },
    ).json()
    assert list_response['ok'] is True
    assert len(list_response['result']['projects']) == 1
    assert list_response['result']['projects'][0]['id'] == source_project_id

    with db_bootstrap.connect() as db:
        rows = db.execute('SELECT id, slug FROM projects ORDER BY id').fetchall()
    assert len(rows) == 1
    assert rows[0]['id'] == source_project_id

    workspace_entries = [entry for entry in runtime_env.workspace_projects_root.iterdir() if entry.is_dir()]
    assert len(workspace_entries) == 1
    assert workspace_entries[0].name == source_project['slug']

    assert not list(runtime_env.workspace_projects_root.rglob('.save-staging'))
    assert not list(runtime_env.workspace_projects_root.rglob('.save-backup'))
    assert (source_root / 'project.yaml').read_text(encoding='utf-8') == source_project_yaml_before

    client = TestClient(app)
    created = client.post(
