def test_export_project_success_builds_archive_and_keeps_canonical_storage(runtime_env):
    client = TestClient(app)
    created = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-create-export-success',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'createProject',
            'payload': {'name': 'Export Success'},
        },
    ).json()
    project = created['result']['project']
    project_root = runtime_env.workspace_projects_root / project['slug']

    (project_root / 'metagen' / 'pump.yaml').write_text(
        yaml.safe_dump(
            {
                'kind': 'metagen.component',
                'component': {'id': 'pump', 'name': 'Pump'},
            },
            sort_keys=False,
            allow_unicode=True,
        ),
        encoding='utf-8',
    )
    (project_root / 'generated' / 'artifact.txt').write_text('generated-artifact', encoding='utf-8')

    before_project_yaml = (project_root / 'project.yaml').read_text(encoding='utf-8')
    before_metagen_yaml = (project_root / 'metagen' / 'pump.yaml').read_text(encoding='utf-8')
    before_generated = (project_root / 'generated' / 'artifact.txt').read_text(encoding='utf-8')

    export_response = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-export-success',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'exportProject',
            'payload': {'projectId': project['id']},
        },
    ).json()

    assert export_response['ok'] is True
    export_result = export_response['result']
    assert export_result['fileName'] == f"{project['slug']}.zip"
    assert export_result['downloadUrl'].startswith('/api/project-exports/')
    assert export_result['exportToken']
    artifact_path = runtime_env.workspace_project_exports_root / f"{export_result['exportToken']}.zip"
    assert artifact_path.exists()
    assert export_result['exportToken'] in command_dispatcher.project_storage_service._project_export_artifacts

    download_response = client.get(export_result['downloadUrl'])
    assert download_response.status_code == 200
    assert download_response.headers.get('content-type', '').startswith('application/zip')

    archive = zipfile.ZipFile(io.BytesIO(download_response.content))
    archived_names = set(archive.namelist())
    assert 'project.yaml' in archived_names
    assert 'metagen/' in archived_names
    assert 'metalab/' in archived_names
    assert 'metaview/' in archived_names
    assert 'generated/' in archived_names
    assert 'metagen/pump.yaml' in archived_names
    assert 'generated/artifact.txt' in archived_names
    assert yaml.safe_load(archive.read('project.yaml').decode('utf-8'))['project']['id'] == project['id']
    assert archive.read('generated/artifact.txt').decode('utf-8') == 'generated-artifact'

    token_reuse_response = client.get(export_result['downloadUrl'])
    assert token_reuse_response.status_code == 404
    assert not artifact_path.exists()
    assert export_result['exportToken'] not in command_dispatcher.project_storage_service._project_export_artifacts

    assert (project_root / 'project.yaml').read_text(encoding='utf-8') == before_project_yaml
    assert (project_root / 'metagen' / 'pump.yaml').read_text(encoding='utf-8') == before_metagen_yaml
    assert (project_root / 'generated' / 'artifact.txt').read_text(encoding='utf-8') == before_generated
    assert not list(runtime_env.workspace_projects_root.rglob('.save-staging'))
    assert not list(runtime_env.workspace_projects_root.rglob('.save-backup'))


def test_export_project_prunes_stale_unconsumed_artifacts_on_next_export(runtime_env, monkeypatch):
    client = TestClient(app)
    created = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-create-export-prune',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'createProject',
            'payload': {'name': 'Export Prune'},
        },
    ).json()
    project = created['result']['project']
    initial_now = 1_700_000_000
    max_age = project_storage.PROJECT_EXPORT_ARTIFACT_MAX_AGE_SECONDS

    monkeypatch.setattr(project_storage.time, 'time', lambda: initial_now)
    first_export = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-export-prune-first',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'exportProject',
            'payload': {'projectId': project['id']},
        },
    ).json()
    assert first_export['ok'] is True
    first_token = first_export['result']['exportToken']
    first_artifact_path = runtime_env.workspace_project_exports_root / f'{first_token}.zip'
    assert first_artifact_path.exists()
    assert first_token in command_dispatcher.project_storage_service._project_export_artifacts

    monkeypatch.setattr(project_storage.time, 'time', lambda: initial_now + max_age + 1)
    second_export = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-export-prune-second',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'exportProject',
            'payload': {'projectId': project['id']},
        },
    ).json()
    assert second_export['ok'] is True
    second_token = second_export['result']['exportToken']

    assert second_token in command_dispatcher.project_storage_service._project_export_artifacts
    assert first_token not in command_dispatcher.project_storage_service._project_export_artifacts
    assert not first_artifact_path.exists()


def test_export_project_consume_missing_artifact_returns_404_and_cleans_registry(runtime_env):
    client = TestClient(app)
    created = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-create-export-missing-artifact',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'createProject',
            'payload': {'name': 'Export Missing Artifact'},
        },
    ).json()
    project = created['result']['project']

    export_response = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-export-missing-artifact',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'exportProject',
            'payload': {'projectId': project['id']},
        },
    ).json()
    assert export_response['ok'] is True
    export_token = export_response['result']['exportToken']
    artifact_path = runtime_env.workspace_project_exports_root / f'{export_token}.zip'
    assert artifact_path.exists()
    assert export_token in command_dispatcher.project_storage_service._project_export_artifacts

    artifact_path.unlink(missing_ok=True)
    download_response = client.get(export_response['result']['downloadUrl'])
    assert download_response.status_code == 404
    assert export_token not in command_dispatcher.project_storage_service._project_export_artifacts


def test_export_project_download_with_unknown_token_returns_404(runtime_env):
    client = TestClient(app)
    response = client.get('/api/project-exports/export_unknown')

    assert response.status_code == 404
    assert response.json()['detail'] == 'Project export not found'


def test_export_project_missing_returns_project_not_found(runtime_env):
    client = TestClient(app)
    response = client.post(
        API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
        json={
            'requestId': 'req-export-missing',
            'module': 'platform',
            'command': 'exportProject',
            'payload': {'projectId': 'missing-project'},
        },
    )

    body = response.json()
    assert body['ok'] is False
    assert body['error']['code'] == 'PROJECT_NOT_FOUND'
    assert body['error']['details']['projectId'] == 'missing-project'


==================================================
FILE: runtime_backend/tests/test_startup_probe.py
==================================================

import json
import socket
import subprocess
import sys
import time
from urllib import error, request

import pytest

from runtime_backend.app.core.constants import API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT

CANONICAL_PYTEST_COMMAND = 'python -m pytest runtime_backend/tests -q'
CANONICAL_STARTUP_TARGET = 'runtime_backend.app.main:app'
CANONICAL_STARTUP_ARGS = [
    sys.executable,
    '-m',
    'uvicorn',
    CANONICAL_STARTUP_TARGET,
    '--host',
    '127.0.0.1',
    '--port',
    '8000',
    '--log-level',
    'warning',
]
STARTUP_TIMEOUT_SECONDS = 12


def _is_tcp_port_in_use(host: str, port: int) -> bool:
    with socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM) as probe:
        probe.settimeout(0.2)
        return probe.connect_ex((host, port)) == 0


def _wait_for_http_ready(url: str, timeout_seconds: int) -> bool:
    deadline = time.time() + timeout_seconds
    while time.time() < deadline:
        try:
            with request.urlopen(url, timeout=0.5) as response:
                if response.status == 200:
                    return True
        except (error.URLError, TimeoutError):
            time.sleep(0.15)
    return False


def test_verification_policy_constants_are_explicit():
    assert CANONICAL_PYTEST_COMMAND == 'python -m pytest runtime_backend/tests -q'
    assert CANONICAL_STARTUP_TARGET == 'runtime_backend.app.main:app'
    assert CANONICAL_STARTUP_ARGS[0] == sys.executable
    assert CANONICAL_STARTUP_ARGS[1:4] == ['-m', 'uvicorn', CANONICAL_STARTUP_TARGET]
    assert '--host' in CANONICAL_STARTUP_ARGS
    assert '--port' in CANONICAL_STARTUP_ARGS


def test_bounded_uvicorn_startup_probe_starts_and_stops_cleanly():
    if _is_tcp_port_in_use('127.0.0.1', 8000):
        pytest.skip('Port 8000 is already in use; bounded startup probe requires the canonical port.')

    process = subprocess.Popen(
        CANONICAL_STARTUP_ARGS,
        stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
        stderr=subprocess.STDOUT,
        text=True,
    )
    try:
        openapi_ready = _wait_for_http_ready('http://127.0.0.1:8000/openapi.json', STARTUP_TIMEOUT_SECONDS)
        assert openapi_ready, 'Uvicorn did not become ready within timeout.'

        payload = json.dumps(
            {
                'requestId': 'probe-list-projects',
                'module': 'platform',
                'command': 'listProjects',
                'payload': {},
            }
        ).encode('utf-8')
        http_request = request.Request(
            f'http://127.0.0.1:8000{API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT}',
            data=payload,
            headers={'Content-Type': 'application/json'},
            method='POST',
        )
        with request.urlopen(http_request, timeout=1.5) as response:
            body = json.loads(response.read().decode('utf-8'))
        assert response.status == 200
        assert body['ok'] is True
    finally:
        process.terminate()
        try:
            process.wait(timeout=5)
        except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
            process.kill()
            process.wait(timeout=5)
